The Daily News stated that we should now make a final effort and unreservedly engage in consolidating the League of Nations Covenant and the more precise sanctions under Article 16, to preserve the League of Nations. The Daily Mail stated that British policy should frankly declare that the British government is determined to focus on British security and immediately build the strongest air force. (10th Reuters Telegram)

Franco-Russian Gentlemen's Agreement Established - Strengthening the League of Nations Covenant's Sanction Clauses - Actually Contains a Military Alliance - Replaces the Eastern European Pact If It Fails 27

(Paris) French Foreign Minister Laval and Soviet Russian Ambassador Potemkin met for two hours today, and have effectively agreed that if Germany and Poland continue to refuse to join the Eastern European Pact, France and Soviet Russia should conclude an agreement to replace it. The agreement is divided into two main parts: (1) Requesting the League of Nations Council to reaffirm and strengthen Articles 10, 16, and 17 of the Covenant; (2) Stipulating the mutual obligations of France and Soviet Russia under these articles.

The Soviet Russian Ambassador invited the diplomatic representatives of Romania, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Greece, and Turkey to a private dinner to exchange opinions on the overall European situation, and then telegraphed People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov, stating that they had approved the agreement. According to reports in the local newspapers, the agreement will eventually take the form of a military agreement and will be integrated with the revision of the League of Nations mechanism and will echo the suggestions made by France at the Stresa conference. France's suggestions include amending the League of Nations Covenant to effectively implement defensive cooperation, control arms limitations, and provide mutual military assistance agreements for countries to join. (9th Reuters Telegram)

Key Points of the Agreement

(Geneva) Foreign Minister Laval and Soviet Russian Ambassador to France, Dankin, jointly agreed on the Franco-Russian agreement yesterday. The content is as follows:

(1) The preamble is based on Articles 10, 16, and 17 of the League of Nations Covenant. Article 17 stipulates the protection of the territorial integrity and political independence of member states, Article 16 stipulates the sanction procedures to be taken when a member state engages in war, and Article 17 stipulates the sanction procedures to be taken when a non-League of Nations member state engages in war. In addition, it also cites the military measures that should be taken under Article 16, Paragraph 2 of the Covenant when a member state engages in war, in order to respect its obligations to the League of Nations (i.e., the Council should suggest to the governments of the countries concerned the effective land, sea, and air forces that each member state should contribute to uphold the Covenant); (2) The two countries endorse the method stipulated in Article 15, Paragraph 7 of the League of Nations Covenant, namely, if the Council is unable to obtain the unanimous acceptance of the report by the member states (excluding the parties to the dispute) attending the Council to resolve the dispute, each member state reserves the right to implement the actions deemed necessary to maintain fairness and justice. This article is based on the foundations recognized by the Locarno Treaties, such as the Franco-Polish Treaty and the Franco-Czech Treaty; (3) In the event of an act of aggression, it shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the League of Nations Covenant, namely, if a member state engages in war, it shall be considered to have committed an act of war against all other member states of the League of Nations in fact. In this special situation, defensive measures may be taken automatically. The above are the main points of the Franco-Russian agreement. As for the technical details, they must be jointly discussed by Laval and Soviet Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov in Geneva before drafting the final text. This agreement is currently only signed by France and Russia. In the future, the Czech Republic and the Soviet Union will conclude a similar agreement. If other countries also adopt this method and conclude agreements with each other, it can become a universal mutual assistance system. (10th Havas Telegram)

Details to be Discussed Later

(Paris) This afternoon, Soviet Russian Ambassador to France Potemkin visited Foreign Minister Laval to discuss the conclusion of the Franco-Russian treaty. The opinions of the two governments on this treaty are already consistent. The various technical details will be discussed in person by Laval and Soviet Commissioner for Foreign Affairs Litvinov in Geneva. When Foreign Minister Laval goes to Russia, this treaty can be formally signed. (9th Havas Telegram)

Paris Newspapers Unanimously Praise 28

(Paris) Today, all Paris newspapers gladly welcomed the proposal that if Germany and Poland refuse to participate in the Eastern European Pact, France and Russia should conclude an agreement to replace it. The newspapers believe that Britain has now recognized Soviet Russia as a component in peaceful work and must praise the increased safety of the new mutual assistance agreement for Britain’s position in Asia. At the same time, France is currently speculating about the attitude that Britain will take at the Stresa conference. The newspapers believe that Italy's determined proposals at the Stresa conference are consistent with France's inclinations, and that Britain's trends will integrate with these trends. Le Petit Journal said that if the British delegation saw that a system based on the League of Nations cannot be established and that military alliances will inevitably be concluded to replace it, it would resolutely announce its support for this system. (10th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) This morning, various newspapers rushed to report that France and Soviet Russia have agreed on the principle of a "gentlemen's agreement." Le Journal and L'Écho de Paris reported on a military treaty based on Articles 10, 16, and 17 of the League of Nations Covenant, which will be signed after the Stresa conference and the League of Nations Council meeting this month in China. Le Journal stated that its details have not yet been drafted, but the principles have been agreed upon by both parties. The Eastern European Pact will become a military treaty, but it is still based on the League of Nations. The newspaper also commented on the regeneration of the League of Nations, saying that after this agreement is concluded, the League of Nations will be able to punish aggressor nations with rapid and practical automatic sanctions. France plans to stipulate arms limitations and use military treaties as guarantees. The Eastern European Pact will be signed first, containing compulsory military assistance, and all countries can participate. The French government also suggested amending Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant. L'Aube believes that the first step of the Eastern European Pact is to create a line of encirclement around Germany, while L'Écho de Paris stated that a Central European Pact will be concluded based on the same principles. Le Matin, regarding the amendment of Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, stated that the League of Nations was unable to decide who the aggressors were, and that automatic assistance would only take effect after the various countries restored their freedom of action. (10th National Telegram)

Geneva Considers it a Clever Action 29

(Geneva) Here, the agreement that France and Russia negotiated and decided to formulate yesterday is regarded as a very clever action, which can have a very important impact at the Stresa conference. This move is intended to make the empty articles of the League of Nations Covenant effective. It seems that Italy will follow in France's footsteps. If so, the League of Nations Council meeting on April 15 will inevitably develop an interesting situation, and will put the British delegation in an unpleasant position. The artifice of consolidating the League of Nations by interpreting Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant based on mutual assistance will gain the powerful support of the Balkan Entente countries, the Little Entente countries, and the countries of the Scandinavian Peninsula. (10th Reuters Telegram)

League of Nations Covenant Article 10: The Members of the League undertake to respect and preserve as against external aggression the territorial integrity and existing political independence of all Members of the League. In case of any such aggression or in case of any threat or danger of such aggression the Council shall advise upon the means by which this obligation shall be fulfilled.

Article 16: Should any Member of the League resort to war in disregard of its covenants under Articles 12, 13 or 15, it shall ipso facto be deemed to have committed an act of war against all other Members of the League, which hereby undertake immediately to subject it to the severance of all trade or financial relations, the prohibition of all intercourse between their nationals and the nationals of the covenant-breaking State, and the prevention of all financial, commercial or personal intercourse between the nationals of the covenant-breaking State and the nationals of any other State, whether a Member of the League or not. It shall be the duty of the Council in such case to recommend to the several governments concerned what effective military, naval or air force the Members of the League shall severally contribute to the armed forces to be used to protect the covenants of the League.

The Members of the League agree, further, that they will mutually support one another in the financial and economic measures which are taken under this Article, in order to minimise the loss and inconvenience resulting therefrom, and that they will mutually support one another in resisting any special measures aimed at one of their number by the covenant-breaking State, and that they will take the necessary steps to afford passage through their territory to the forces of any of the Members of the League which are co-operating to protect the covenants of the League.

Any Member of the League which has violated any covenant of the League may be declared to be no longer a Member of the League by a vote of the Council concurred in by the Representatives of all the other Members of the League represented thereon.

Article 17: In the event of a dispute between a Member of the League and a State which is not a Member of the League, or between States not Members of the League, the State or States not Members of the League shall be invited to accept the obligations of membership in the League for the purposes of such dispute, upon such conditions as the Council may deem just. If such invitation is accepted, the provisions of Articles 12 to 16 inclusive shall be applied with such modifications as may be deemed necessary by the Council.

Upon such invitation being given the Council shall immediately institute an inquiry into the circumstances of the dispute and recommend such action as may seem best and most effectual in the circumstances.

If a State so invited shall refuse to accept the obligations of membership in the League for the purposes of such dispute, and shall resort to war against a Member of the League, the provisions of Article 16 shall be applicable as against the State taking such action.

If both parties to the dispute when so invited refuse to accept the obligations of membership in the League for the purposes of such dispute, the Council may take such measures and make such recommendations as will prevent hostilities and will result in the settlement of the dispute.

Special Meeting of the League of Nations This Month on the 15th 30

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council is scheduled to hold an emergency meeting next week, i.e., on April 15, chaired by Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü Aras, to discuss the issue of German rearmament at the request of the French government. (10th Havas Telegram)

French Cabinet Authorizes Two Representatives to Freely Conclude Conventions - Memorandum to the League of Nations Passed 31

(Paris) The French cabinet met for three hours last night and decided to grant Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval the authority to freely conclude non-aggression and mutual assistance conventions at the Stresa conference. The Stresa conference will open tomorrow. This convention will stipulate automatic military and economic adjudication to punish countries that disrupt European peace. According to reliable sources here, the Soviet Russian government supports the French plan, namely, that the signatory countries to this convention will meet anytime, anywhere, outside of Geneva in the event of a sudden attack, and decide on actions. According to the opinions of Soviet Russia and France, if this plan is passed by the Stresa conference, negotiations will still be carried out within the structure of the League of Nations. Officials declared before the French representatives departed that when Foreign Minister Laval comes to Moscow to visit, in addition to signing a general agreement within the scope of the League of Nations with Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov, he will also conclude a Franco-Russian mutual assistance convention. According to a telegram from Rome, Prime Minister Mussolini does not want to have any concrete expressions before the opening of the Stresa conference. (10th National Telegram)

(Paris) Today's cabinet meeting passed the French memorandum and draft resolution submitted to the League of Nations Council regarding the issue of German rearmament (for details, see our telegram on the 7th). This draft resolution will first be discussed by the Stresa three-nation conference. The French government hopes that this draft resolution can be submitted to the Council meeting jointly with Britain and Italy. British Foreign Secretary Discloses Contents of Berlin Talks to the House of Commons 34

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon today gave a speech in the House of Commons, revealing for the first time the details of Germany's request for expansion of its army, navy, and air force. Simon stated that German leader Hitler recently suggested during talks with him in Berlin that he wanted to equip the army with thirty-six divisions totaling 550,000 men, and also demanded that Germany should have weapons equal to those of other countries. As for the navy and air force, with some reservations, Germany requested that its navy's total tonnage should be equal to 35% of Britain's, and its air force should be equal to that of Britain and France. Germany is prepared to accept a military inspection system, but only on the condition that all countries accept it simultaneously. If Germany's status cannot be equal, then it is still unwilling to return to the League of Nations. Simon also acknowledged for the first time that Hitler had requested the restoration of territories lost in the peace treaty. He also expressed Britain's disappointment to Hitler because the opinions of all parties were difficult to reconcile. As for what measures Britain will take in the Stresa Conference, the Foreign Secretary said that the government has not yet determined its attitude towards the talks that Lord Privy Seal Eden had in the capitals of various European countries. Germany has made it clear that it is unwilling to participate in the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, and even less willing to participate with Russia. However, Germany is willing to join if countries related to the Eastern European issue sign non-aggression treaties stipulating mutual consultation in the event of a risk of aggression. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon today briefly outlined in the House of Commons the talks he and Eden had in Berlin, and the talks Eden later had in Moscow, Warsaw, and Prague.

Germany Opposes Eastern European Pact: Says Hitler told him that Germany does not want to sign an Eastern European Pact containing mutual assistance and including Lithuania in any non-aggression pact, and especially opposes concluding a mutual assistance agreement with Soviet Russia. He advocates that countries involved in the Eastern European issue should conclude non-aggression pacts, with clauses attached for mutual consultation in the event of aggression.

No Objection to Central European Pact: Although Hitler has no objection to the Central European Pact, it is expected that great difficulties will arise regarding the clause that it will not interfere in German-Austrian relations. However, Germany is prepared to consider this issue when other governments reach a compromise on the establishment of this pact.

Requests Expansion of Army, Navy, and Air Force: Mr. Hitler also said that Germany must have thirty-six divisions, with a maximum troop strength of 550,000 men, including one division of the National Socialist Party's guards and armed police. He also said that Germany currently has all kinds of weapons that other countries have, and if a certain country stops manufacturing a certain weapon, then Germany does not want to manufacture it either. Later, regarding the naval issue, Mr. Hitler requested that Germany must have at least 35% of Britain's tonnage. As for the air force, if Soviet Russia's air force does not change, then the air forces of Britain, France, and Germany must be equal.

Does Not Forget Old Territories: Germany agrees to the Sky Pact under discussion. Germany is willing to make an agreement on the limitation of armaments that contains prohibition, but this kind of agreement must be applied equally to all countries. Mr. Hitler also told him that if Germany is placed in a position of inferiority for a long time, then it does not want to participate in the work of the League of Nations. Germany currently has no colonies, which is one aspect of its inferior status. He and Eden did not approve of certain opinions expressed by Hitler and German cabinet members regarding certain points. When the talks were over, he stated to Hitler that it was disappointing that such great difficulties had arisen in reaching a compromise.

Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia's Positions: Simon continued, saying that Eden had learned in Moscow that the Soviet Russian government was willing to promote a European security system based on the principles of the League of Nations as planned in the London Communiqué of February 3. The Soviet Union had firmly stated that the Eastern European Pact was not intended to encircle any country, but to provide equal security for all countries, and believed that the participation of Germany and Poland in the pact was the best solution to the problem. In Warsaw, Eden was explained to by Polish Foreign Minister Beck that Poland must maintain a state of tranquility on the borders of Germany and Russia through existing treaties, and asked whether any new proposals would enhance or disturb the tranquility that had already been achieved. Beck and Czech Foreign Minister Beneš both hoped that the Stresa Conference would advance the Central European Pact and lead to its establishment.

Simon concluded by saying that the Stresa Conference will be followed by a meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council convened by France next Monday. Simon refused to make any statements regarding the government's foreign policy before the Stresa Conference, but Prime Minister MacDonald has agreed to choose a day in the House of Commons after the Easter holiday to debate foreign affairs (Reuters, 9th).

German Military and Civilians Celebrate Together, Ludendorff's Inspiring Words: Spirit of Sacrifice is the Source of Self-Defense, Universal Military Service is the Foundation of Survival 39

Munich Today is the 70th birthday of Ludendorff, the only surviving old general in Germany. His former subordinates gathered at Ludendorff's villa near Munich to hold a parade in celebration. Since 8:00 AM, more than 2,000 people gathered near Ludendorff's villa, many of whom were retired officers wearing the German military uniforms from before the European War. Before long, the current Army Minister von Blomberg and Army Commander-in-Chief von Fritsch also arrived to congratulate Ludendorff. General von Blomberg then addressed the crowd, saying that Germany has now implemented conscription, so the organization of the new German army is closer to the old military system before the war. The old German army, both before the war and during the European War, was trained and guided by Ludendorff, and the new army in the future will also take Ludendorff's spirit as a model. General Ludendorff, wearing his old general's uniform, accepted the salute of the parade participants, standing straight with his chest out, his heroic spirit undiminished from those years. He also gave a brief speech to the public, first thanking them, and then saying that he was honored to wear his old military uniform again. Mr. Ludendorff then recounted the deeds of his old comrades who sacrificed themselves for the country in the European War, saying that their spirit of sacrifice is the source of racial freedom and self-defense, and the cornerstone of today's great nation. Mr. Ludendorff concluded by saying that the country has now implemented conscription, and this universal military service is the foundation of the German people's true survival (National Telegram, 9th).

US Naval Engineering Project Passed by Both Houses, Now Awaiting President Roosevelt's Signature. Expansion of Standing Army Act Already Signed by President. House of Representatives Re-Passes the War Profits Cancellation Act 43

(Washington) The Naval Engineering Program Act, which was passed by the House of Representatives on March 27, was passed by the Senate today and is now being sent to President Roosevelt for signature. The act stipulates naval engineering funds of 38 million US dollars, of which 26 million US dollars will be used for naval bases on the west coast and Pearl Harbor in Hawaii, and 10 million US dollars will be used to build floating docks. In addition, several million US dollars are needed to build a submarine base and powder magazine in the Panama Canal Zone (Reuters, 9th).

(Washington) The Army Budget Act for the current fiscal year, which lists expenditures of $401,998,170 and approves a 40% increase in the size of the standing army, from 118,700 to 165,000, was previously passed by both the House and Senate and has now been signed into law by President Roosevelt (Havas, 9th).

(Washington) The House of Representatives today passed McKissick's War Profits Cancellation Act, giving the god of war a major blow in the United States. The act passed by a vote of 365 to 15. Beforehand, opponents of the original proposal had forced the Military Affairs Committee to delete the point authorizing the President to implement conscription during wartime. However, according to the current form passed, the President still has broad powers to requisition domestic manpower and financial resources. In addition to being able to tax excessive war profits at 100%, the act also has the following points: (1) After the United States declares war, the government can control all prices. (2) All industries must apply for licenses during wartime, and the distribution of major goods must be managed by the government. (3) It is forbidden to send American people to any foreign country to fight, except in cases where the United States is in danger of being invaded. (4) The President is authorized to order the suspension of operations of all domestic securities and commodities exchanges when necessary. The act has now been sent to the Senate, which is planning to add further restrictions. The Senate Munitions Investigating Committee is also studying limiting war profits for ordinary businesses to no more than 3% of the original capital. For personal war profits, the Senate may limit each person to no more than 8,000 US dollars per year. The army opposes this drastic move, fearing that munitions merchants' capital will★■■■★■■★■■★★, and reconciliation between the two sides may be quite difficult. In addition, the Senate also introduced a bill on wartime today. The proposers are Republican Knight and Democratic Clark. Knight's proposal advocates authorizing the President to refuse to issue passports to American people for travel abroad during wartime. Clark's proposal stipulates that anyone who lends money to belligerent countries to enable them to purchase goods should be sentenced to imprisonment and heavy fines (National News Agency, 9th).

Initial Draft of Bankruptcy Law Announced 50

(Nanjing) The initial draft of the Bankruptcy Law of the Republic of China, drafted by the Civil Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan, has been completed, with a total of four chapters, ten sections, and 160 articles. It was announced on the afternoon of the 10th to solicit opinions, with a deadline of May 10th, and will be submitted to the General Assembly for discussion in June. The main points of the law include: (1) The cause of bankruptcy adopts a comprehensive doctrine. (2) The declaration of bankruptcy adopts the application doctrine. (3) The bankruptcy estate adopts the expansion doctrine. (4) Reconciliation and bankruptcy cases are exclusively under the jurisdiction of the court where the debtor's or bankrupt's business is located. If there is no business location, the court where the debtor resides has jurisdiction. (5) A request for reconciliation must be approved or rejected before a bankruptcy request is made, and is made by a ruling that cannot be appealed. (6) The terms of reconciliation are freely negotiated by the debtor and creditors, and there are no strengthened regulations on the number and timing of repayments. If the debtor has malicious intent, they will not be allowed to enjoy the benefits of reconciliation. (7) If a bankruptcy creditor has been reduced in repayment through conciliation or bankruptcy proceedings, the part of the debt that has not been repaid is deemed to be extinguished. (8) Debtors who commit fraud in reconciliation, bankrupts who commit fraud in bankruptcy, or who have committed specific criminal acts within one year before bankruptcy, or who do not fulfill specific obligations prescribed by this law or commit fraudulent acts during the bankruptcy proceedings, shall be punished. According to the Chairman of the Civil Law Committee, Fu Bingchang, the points in which this law differs from the bankruptcy laws of various countries include: (1) German bankruptcy law is a pure law, while this is a cooperative civil and commercial bankruptcy law. (2) It maintains our country's inherent good habits. The main points are: A. Reconciliation allows the application of courts or chambers of commerce. Reconciliation is handled with the consent of both parties. B. The bankruptcy law of each country stipulates that debt distribution adopts a proportional method, while this law adopts a situational domination. C. It distinguishes between good-faith bankruptcy and malicious bankruptcy. Those who are in good faith because the reason is unfortunate are slightly forgiven, while those who are in bad faith have strict measures to punish them. As for the previous remaining debts, in the bankruptcy laws of various countries, such as Germany, when the judgment is made, in addition to the bankrupt then liquidating their existing payments to the creditors, a certificate must be issued for the remaining debts, which is to be collected when the debtor has the ability. The UK also has the same provisions at the time of judgment. This law has already stipulated that when the official announces bankruptcy, it will be liquidated according to the existing ones, so that the bankrupt will have the opportunity and spirit to engage in business again. This law is based on the spirit of civil law and our country's inherent habits and needs, striving for simplicity in order to be applied. During the opinion solicitation period, if all parties have opinions to contribute, they will be especially valued in order to gather the wisdom of the public (Special Dispatch, 10th).

International Commercial Telegram - Special Business Telegram from Reuters on April 10th - 78

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: The gold market continued to fall, with today's price at 143 shillings and 6 pence, 7.5 pence lower than yesterday. The London silver market rose 125 points today. The spot price is 28.9375 pence, and the futures price is 29.0625 pence. Speculators and India bought in the morning, and China also bought in, but then sold. The closing market was stable.

Bombay Silver Market: The market opened slightly lower today, improved in the afternoon, and the closing sentiment was firm. The spot price is 68 rupees and 11 annas, an increase of 4 annas.

Exchange Rates

Sterling vs. US Dollar: In the London foreign exchange market, the pound rose today due to good demand. The market opened strong and fluctuated little afterwards. The market was quite active, and trading was good. The opening price of the sterling-dollar exchange rate was $4.85125, 1.125 points higher than yesterday's closing price. It rose half a point at 11:00, fell 25 points at noon to $4.85375, rose 125 points at 1:00 PM, fell 25 points at 2:00 PM to $4.8525, 125 points higher than the opening price.

Sterling vs. French Franc: The market opened with a rise of 18 points to 73.59 francs. It further rose 10 points at 11:00. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, following the fall in the sterling-dollar exchange rate, it fell to the opening price of 73.59 francs.

US Dollar vs. Sterling: The New York foreign exchange market was stable today. The sterling exchange rate was $4.85125, an increase of 1.125 points.

US Dollar vs. French Franc: The US dollar-French franc exchange rate remained unchanged at 6.5925.

US Dollar vs. Dutch Guilder: The US dollar-Dutch guilder exchange rate rose 1 point to 67.45.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: The cotton market opened with a price increase of 2.5 cents per bale, because the government will provide credit facilities for the export industry. It is said that the government's cotton policy seems to be showing signs of change. The continuation of loans and the abolition of continued donations will soon be clear. After the Reconstruction and Industrialization Loan (工振案) is signed, it will definitely have a good impact on the cotton market.

Bombay Cotton: The market closed yesterday afternoon and did not open today because the US cotton exchange was searched by the police for gambling on US cotton futures yesterday.

Liverpool Cotton: At 1:00 PM this afternoon, the July futures price was 6.24, an increase of 5 points.

Liverpool Wheat: At 1:00 PM this afternoon, the July futures price was 5 shillings and 7.375 pence, 0.875 points higher than yesterday's closing price.

Chicago Wheat: The market opened this morning with an increase of about 1 point due to unfavorable weather reports and rumors of recurring sandstorms. Winnipeg wheat prices were lower.

Rubber

London: The rubber market opened more stable, and prices were slightly higher, then turned quiet. The opening transaction price for July-September futures was 5.6875 pence, unchanged until noon. The later market developed slightly.

New York: Strike news still dominates the rubber market. Although strike news improved this morning, and the London telegrams were also good, the price of July rubber futures fell 15 points at the opening today. The sentiment stabilized after the price drop, and transactions were light.

Securities

New York: Before the opening of securities today, Wall Street sentiment was generally bullish. The rebound since last night is expected to unfold today, because the time for the government to announce the use of its Reconstruction and Industrialization Loan (工振案) mega-project is not far away. At the same time, the news about the rubber tire workers' strike has indeed improved. The meeting between the Ministry of Labor and the Federation of Labor is likely to achieve satisfactory results. Mutual concessions may be possible before the strike is realized. The railway situation has also improved. All these news have a good impact on the market. When the securities market opened this morning, most prices were unchanged, with occasional slight increases, mostly limited to fractional numbers. Trading was still active in the first half hour, then fell. After an hour, most of the opening prices could still be maintained, but the sentiment was not very strong. In the Midst of Inflation, the Understanding We Should Have 79

Since the financial panic last year in our country, the sound of inflation has been very loud in the market. At the end of last month, after the government issued 100 million yuan in financial bonds, this sound became even louder, causing the bidding price to skyrocket. Those who own assets either hoard cash or try to exchange for goods to avoid the worry of freezing and starvation, spending their days in fear. After the Ministry of Finance dispelled the rumors, this trend subsided slightly. It can be said that the masses were troubling themselves unnecessarily. It is important to know that in our country's current situation, there is no possibility of adopting new policies. However, the concentration of floating capital in cities without engaging in production is ultimately not a blessing for the country. Occasionally, those who are interested in production enterprises are often troubled by not knowing the tricks and having difficulty in designing, selecting, purchasing, installing, and managing machinery, which leads to interruptions. In fact, if a certain production enterprise is determined, there are already agencies in the country that can handle the above-mentioned problems, such as:

The Shanghai Tongji Engineering Company is organized by experts in various fields of engineering and specializes in solving the above-mentioned problems for domestic industrialists. It has been in operation for four years, and it has handled countless cases in various provinces and cities. It is diligent in its work and has a very good reputation. Therefore, the products of government agencies such as the Engineering Research Institute of the Academia Sinica, the Electrical Machinery Manufacturing Plant of the Construction Committee, and businesses such as the Housheng Machinery Factory are all entrusted to it as the exclusive manager. Recently, it is undertaking the entire machinery project of the Sichuan Kaiji Alkali Manufacturing Company, the weaving workshop of the Shou County Women's Vocational School in Anhui, and the large and small cabinet projects of the Gongxian Arsenal Branch Factory, which are quite busy. Those interested in production enterprises who entrust the entire project, design, etc., can avoid all difficulties and achieve satisfactory results.

The Northeast After the Conclusion of the Sino-Soviet Railway Deal 99

— (Changchun Correspondence)

After a year and nine months of repeated negotiations and countless twists and turns between Japan and the Soviet Union regarding the sale of the Sino-Soviet Railway, a formal agreement has finally been signed. Moreover, the first installment of 23.3 million Japanese yen was received on the day of the signing. The remaining payments are scheduled to be made in installments. Most of the important Soviet personnel on the Sino-Soviet Railway are preparing to hand over their positions, and their families have already returned to their home country. The number of Soviet personnel on the railway is approximately 7,000, and the first batch of Japanese personnel sent to take over amounts to 5,000. Although it is currently said that as long as they are willing to work diligently and do not hinder the so-called "Manchukuo," they can continue to stay, in reality, it is feared that it will be difficult to allow their continued presence. Not only will it be difficult for the majority of Soviet railway employees to remain, but also many of the ordinary Soviet merchants, totaling more than 35,000, will have to pack their bags and return home. Although the influence of the Soviet Union in the Northeast may not be completely eliminated, at least it will no longer be able to control the real economic power of the Northeast. In the future, it will be in a passive position. The area surrounded by the Songhua and Nen Rivers is the richest region, with approximately 87.22 million hectares of arable land. Currently, only about 20% of this land has been cultivated, which is only 17.8 million hectares. This area is the largest source of revenue for the Sino-Soviet Railway and the most important region of the Northeast. In terms of production, considering only agricultural products, soybeans account for about 36%, millet for 20%, sorghum for 15%, wheat for 12%, and corn for 7%. In short, the Northeast's special products largely come from the Northeast region. Although the Greater and Lesser Khingan Ranges are undeveloped and unsuitable for cultivation, they contain ancient, untouched forests covering at least 190,000 to 200,000 square kilometers, with timber reserves exceeding 100 million cubic feet. The tree species include coniferous trees such as Korean pine, Ezo spruce, fir, and larch, as well as broad-leaved trees such as mountain pear, bodhi, poplar, cottonwood, Qinggang oak, and birch. Currently, logging is mostly concentrated near Jilin and along the Sino-Soviet Railway, accounting for only about 10% of the total forest area.

Animal husbandry is also very promising. The areas related to the Sino-Soviet Railway have a total of 9 million head of sheep and horses. The central region for animal husbandry is the Hulunbuir area. The quality of the wool is very good, and the developing Japanese wool industry has a particular need for wool from this area. Currently, the trading centers for livestock hides and furs are Qiqihar, Hailar, and Manchuria. Exports are mostly concentrated in Vladivostok. Now that the Sino-Soviet Railway is under Japanese control, these globally traded items will be exported eastward to Chongjin and absorbed westward by Dalian.

The Northeast is also rich in mineral resources. In terms of those already mined, Zhalainuoer produces lignite. The coal produced in Muling, Heligang, Mishan, Dongning, Ganhe, and other places is of excellent quality, not inferior to the products of Fushun. The reserves in these locations alone amount to 250 million tons. According to a certain expert's survey, the coal reserves in the Northeast are at least 30 billion tons (approximately one-third of the total coal reserves in Japan). Of particular interest is placer gold. The main streams and tributaries of the Ergune River in Heilongjiang all produce considerable quantities, which is also urgently needed by Japan. Although the reserves of other mineral resources such as silver, copper, lead, and aluminum have not been clearly investigated, they are not insignificant. The salt lake reserves in the Hulunbuir area are even more abundant, truly "inexhaustible." The Northeast's natural resources are richer than those in South Manchuria. Now that the Japanese have succeeded in the transfer of the Sino-Soviet Railway, they can freely exploit them.

Since the September 18th Incident, Japan's railway encroachment in Manchuria has achieved alarming success. Now that the Sino-Soviet Railway has been sold, it will naturally gain even more momentum. However, on the other hand, the industries run by local people are in a slump. For example, the weaving industry in Harbin has almost completely shut down. Previously, there were more than 150 domestic factories in Harbin, with an annual output value of approximately 10 million. Now, only about 30 factories continue to operate, and they are all in a state of anxiety, unable to continue. Seeing such abundant resources being taken over by others while they themselves are starving and freezing, people here feel that it will be even more difficult to run businesses after the Sino-Soviet Railway deal is concluded. (March 28th, Changchun)

Amidst Talk of Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation, Jilin Timber is Imported into China. Tianjin Alone Needs 300,000 Piculs Annually; Illegal Timber Businesses are Active. 100

Changchun Correspondence: Amidst talk of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, the economic relationship between North China and the puppet state, centered on Tianjin, is gradually becoming closer. In the past year, more than 1,000 carts of mats have been imported from the Tangshan area to the puppet state. There has also been a considerable increase in millet and wheat from Shanxi and Chahar. Starting this year, Jilin timber has gradually been imported into North China, showing a significant upward trend. Since the September 18th Incident, most of the construction timber in North China has been imported from coastal areas of the Soviet Union. Recently, due to construction in the Soviet Union, timber imports to North China have gradually decreased. Jilin timber has taken this opportunity to enter the market and is gradually becoming popular. Currently, there are ongoing discussions between the Jilin Timber Industry and the Tianjin Timber Association, planning to import Jilin timber into North China in large quantities. It is estimated that Tianjin alone needs about 300,000 piculs per year. The progress of this trade is currently attracting the attention of those involved. (Northeast News Agency)

The Reorganization of Wang Bingxiao's Unit of the Yutian Militia 101

Beiping Correspondence: Before the Security Team under Feng Shoupeng and others in Yutian County were transferred for reorganization, incidents of discord occurred repeatedly between the team and the local illegal militia. The local people suffered terribly. The destruction was particularly severe in the battle of Yuhong Bridge. Therefore, the residents of the county, especially those who were well-off, completely abandoned their homes and fled. The shops in the suburbs also closed one after another, making it almost a dead city. The authorities, intending to punish the team, contacted the Japanese through the Jiji Mi District Commissioner and the "War Zone Cleanup Committee." After a year of effort, the team was finally transferred for reorganization. Except for those who fled with their weapons, the rest are still able to maintain order. As for the reorganization of the illegal militia in Yutian, it must also be carried out. When Yin Rugeng was in charge of this matter in Yutian, in addition to those who had been disbanded in accordance with the order, the Wang Chengzhu unit and the Wang Bingxiao unit of the Yuhong Bridge militia stubbornly refused to comply. In particular, the Wang Chengzhu unit was the most unruly. They had opened fire with the Zhou Yuying unit of the Security Team. Due to the disparity in numbers and the terrain, they led their troops to break through and flee to the territory of Zunhua County. Wang Chengzhu himself was later captured by the militia in that county and sent back to Yutian. The remnants who fled into Zunhua are still stubbornly resisting in the Liuxing Ridge Mountains, with about 300 people and complete weapons. However, due to the tight encirclement by the Security Team and the militia, they have no way to break through. According to a telephone call from Zunhua this morning (6th), the rebel group originally intended to flee south to Qian'an, but since they cannot succeed, they are now planning to flee to the outside of the pass. Wang Bingxiao took the initiative to express to County Magistrate Zhao and Team Leader Zhou last night (5th) that he was willing to comply with the order for reorganization. This morning (6th), he began to disband. Zhao and Zhou immediately reported to the public office and the provincial government this afternoon (6th). After the unit is resolved, the reorganization of the illegal militia in Yutian County can be considered to have come to an end. (6th)

The Joint Petition of Patrol Police in Luodian, Baoshan 102

Zhou Jintang, the chief of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau in Luodian Town, Baoshan County, took office on the 8th of this month. Unexpectedly, after Chief Zhou took office, he dismissed all the existing police chiefs Zhou Fan and all the more than 20 police officers, and replaced them with new police officers brought by Chief Zhou. After being dismissed, the old police officers, considering that they were still in training, were suddenly dismissed and their livelihoods were precarious. Yesterday (10th), they prepared a document to petition various agencies such as the district party headquarters, the district office, and the chamber of commerce. They also decided to jointly petition the county party headquarters and the county government this morning, requesting that the director be ordered to withdraw the dismissal order.

The Sudden Liquidation of Two Major Firms in Taicang 103

Fuda Money Exchange and Wanquanyu Tongji Sauce Garden in this city were founded by Jiang Yongfan and Jiang Jingsheng, who have been in business for more than ten years. Because the Jiang brothers are honest and prudent, Fuda Money Exchange has a particularly large amount of deposits. Wanquanyu Tongji Sauce Garden also has a considerable number of small depositors. In recent years, the garden has established many branches in Gongji, Heji, Yiji, Yongji, and Zhitang, and its business has been extremely prosperous, holding the leading position in the county's sauce and wine industry. Recently, due to rural bankruptcy and the decline of all industries, Fuda Money Exchange has been unable to maintain its operations due to financial difficulties. Wanquanyu Tongji and its branches have also suffered heavy losses and have been unable to support themselves. Suddenly, at 10:00 AM on the 7th of this month, lawyers Qian Langxi and Wang Kunfu announced the liquidation. The news shocked all sectors. It is reported that the total amount of various creditors is about 400,000 yuan. Jiang Yongfan, who also served as the manager and chairman of Taicang Bank, resigned on the 6th. The bank convened a board meeting that evening and decided to hire Gong Minqiu as the chairman and Shao Menggang as the manager.

The Baby Contest in Zhangyan, Jinshan 104

The Zhangyan People's Education Center in Jinshan, in order to awaken public attention to infant care and health methods and promote children's health, cooperated with various agencies and schools in the town to hold a baby health contest on April 6th. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM on that morning. After Director Xu Xuqin reported the purpose of the meeting and the preparations, the contest began. For a time, plump, lively babies in red and green clothes gathered together, and the audience also flocked in. A total of 97 people participated in the competition, with 6 people who had registered being absent. They were divided into eight stages: 4 to 6 months, 6 months to 1 year, 1 year to 1.5 years, 1.5 years to 2 years, 2 years to 2.5 years, 2.5 years to 3 years, 3 years to 3.5 years, and 3.5 years to 4 years. The competition items were divided into six categories: weight, height, nutrition, posture, facial features, and diseases. Doctors were hired to examine and judge each category. On that day, four stages were held in the morning and four in the afternoon. As a result, Gao Yichou won first place, Liu Jinsheng second place, and Bao Jinlin third place. The award ceremony was held at 9:00 AM on the 7th. The awards were presented by Tu Shunmin, a representative of the Education Bureau, and Yu Shuzhai, the district chief of the Fourth District of Jinshan. The meeting ended at 12:00 noon.

Seven Families Robbed by Bandits in Fengjing Songbang, Songjiang 105

Fengjing Songbang is an area where waterways are divided and bandits roam. Robberies are often heard in the vicinity. At about 2:00 AM on the 6th, more than ten bandits speaking a mixed dialect suddenly came to the area, armed with shoulder poles, knives, and flashlights. They broke into the home of Shen Shaotang and robbed him. Shaotang resisted slightly, and the bandits attacked him in groups, cutting his left forehead, causing blood to flow profusely. They then looted to their hearts' content and went to the homes of Shen Yuanrong, Shen Xiuqin, Shen Jinlian, Shen Guiting, Shen Anqi, and Shen Shaoqin, robbing seven families in a row. For about two hours, they stole a lot of silver, cloth, jewelry, and clothing. The bandits carried their loot and escaped along the original route of Sanxiantang. The victims have each filed a list of losses and reported it to the Second Branch, which has forwarded it to the County Public Security Bureau to request the arrest of the thieves and the recovery of the stolen goods. The injured Shen Shaotang went to seek medical treatment on his own.

The Indictment of the Quan Family Tragedy 106

Quan Lianfu, a resident of Chijiaheng in the west suburbs of this city, abused his daughter-in-law, Ms. Liu, and falsely accused her of infidelity. He incited his son, Quan Wangcai, who was working in Shanghai, to return to Songjiang. Without asking the reason, he beat Ms. Liu, who committed suicide out of resentment. After the family of the deceased, Liu Meichu, reported the case to the bureau and requested the prosecutor's office to examine the injuries, fill out the death certificate, and propose an investigation, it was determined that the defendant Quan Wangcai had caused minor injury to his wife, which constituted a crime under Article 293, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. His coercion caused his wife, Quan Liu, to commit suicide by taking poison, which constituted a suspicion under Article 290, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Also, according to Article 43, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, the defendant Quan Lianfu was suspected of committing the same offense. A public prosecution was filed with the Criminal Court, and a public hearing is scheduled for 9:00 AM on the 13th.

Xie Xia of Suzhou Led a Crowd to Resist Arrest and Assault Police 107

Shuigen, the son of Xie Xia in Caijiawei, Chefang, had a history of hemoptysis. In the first month of this year, he returned home drunk with his neighbors Zhou Agen and Zhou Boying. He fell once on the way. He suddenly died the next day. Xie Xia then filed a complaint with the local court, alleging that Shuigen's death was caused by being beaten by Zhou Agen and others. The court sent prosecutor Yang An and a coroner to the village to examine the body, but there were no injuries. Xie Xia refused to accept this and had the body transported to the city. The court then sent Judge Xia Jinglu and forensic doctor Chen to re-examine the body outside Pingmen, but there were still no injuries. The court then ruled that Zhou Agen and Zhou Boying would not be prosecuted. Afterwards, Xie Xia filed an appeal with the High Court, which was rejected. Unable to vent her anger, she led people to Zhou Boying's house to make trouble from time to time. Zhou Aen and others then filed a counter-suit in court for obstructing freedom. The court repeatedly summoned Xie Xia without success. On the 9th, the court sent bailiffs Zhong Muzi and Hou Jinggui and assistant Zhang Kuaizi, hired a boat to Chefang, and met with the patrol chief and three police officers. Guided by Zhou Yinxiang, Zhou Aen's uncle, they changed boats to Caijiawei to make the arrest. Unexpectedly, as soon as the boat arrived, a crowd of villagers had gathered on the shore. Without asking the reason, they beat and tied up the two bailiffs and one assistant. The public security police and boatmen all fled. Later, boatman Li Gengsheng came to the city on the morning of the 10th to report to the court. The court immediately sent a secretary general to lead bailiffs, accompanied by police officers sent by the Public Security Bureau, to Chefang by speedboat to rescue the two bailiffs and one assistant. It is reported that bailiff Hou Jinggui was the most seriously injured and his life may be in danger. However, Xie Xia suddenly surrendered herself on the afternoon of the 10th. At the same time, Xia Kunquan was arrested outside Fengmen. After interrogation, they were both taken into custody.

The Arrest of the Main Culprit in the Poison Pill Case in Wuxi 108

Zhou Rongquan, a villager in Dunshang Village, Tangtou'an, Er'ertu, Beiting, set up a mechanism to manufacture poison pills at home and made a lot of profit. In July of last year, he was defrauded of more than 1,000 yuan by Changjiao Rongquan and others. Because the spoils were not divided equally, someone reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The village chief Jiang Yingsheng (i.e., Jiang Juchang), who had privately handled the case, and Zheng Chao, who received the money, and Chen Quanfa, the boatman, were arrested and sent to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command. Jiang Yingsheng was sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment, and Zheng Chao and Chen Quanfa were sent back to the original county for retrial. However, the main culprit, Zhou Rongquan, took his wife and children and hid in Suzhou after the incident, living freely under the alias Zhou Shichu, and secretly continued his old business. His manufacturing mechanism had been moved to Mudu in the suburbs of Suzhou (some say outside Kuatang). Zhou himself traveled in and out of Suzhou city and countryside, and his whereabouts were mysterious. The day before yesterday (8th), Zhong Jihe, the detective captain of the Public Security Bureau of this county, learned of the previous situation and sent detectives Yan Zengfu and Wu Zhengrong, the police chief of the county government, to Suzhou to arrest him. Zhou Rongquan was arrested at the entrance of the Wenquan Bathhouse at Shilukou outside Banmen. Eighteen packs of red medicine powder, a roll of cellophane, and more than 300 empty boxes of Butterfly Brand poison pills were found in Zhou's home at No. 151 Qimen Main Street. He was taken to the Third Branch, transferred to the Public Security Bureau for detention, and escorted to Wuxi yesterday for trial.

The Tax Police in Yilin Town, Funing, Oppress the Villagers 109

Jiang Benpu, the captain of the Second Platoon of the tax police stationed in Yilin Town, often used the name of smuggling suppression to send plainclothes teams to Daxu Village in the west of the town, threatening the villagers with guns. Because the banditry was rampant in the area, the villagers were on guard day and night. When they saw this, they suspected that they were bandits and were extremely alarmed. A large number of tax police then arrived, and the villagers began to calm down and requested an investigation. Unexpectedly, the captain ignored them and falsely claimed that the villagers were resisting. He forcibly confiscated five self-defense guns, beat and injured 18 good citizens, including six who were seriously injured, and arrested more than 30 people, extorting huge sums of money. The local villagers were extremely angry. It is reported that they have sent a telegram to the Supervision Office of the Ministry of Finance of the Wuhan Headquarters, requesting strict punishment.

Departed at Noon

Envoy He Left a Photo Before Sailing (Taken by Zhu Shunlin)

Remarks Before Departure

Before his departure, Mr. He told a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency that he would take the Conte Verde to Port Said in Egypt, then change ships to Connie, then take a train for one day. The journey would take a total of 27 days. It is expected that he will arrive in Ankara around the 7th of next month. He recently received a telegram from Wang Zisheng, the counselor of the embassy who had arrived in Ankara earlier, saying that the embassy site and internal arrangements had been largely prepared. The credentials will be carried with him on this trip and can be presented in the middle of next month. He is looking forward to arriving in Turkey to make arrangements.

Will Meet Turkish Envoy

According to those close to Mr. He, after Mr. He takes office, in addition to meeting with the Turkish foreign affairs authorities and President Kemal, and presenting his credentials, he will, if there is an opportunity after arriving in Turkey, first meet with former Turkish Envoy to China, Sir Fubpei. Sir Fubpei was the first Turkish charge d'affaires to China and was promoted to envoy. Four years ago, there was an embassy in Shanghai, but it was canceled due to Turkey's implementation of a downsizing policy. It is not known who will be sent when it is restored in the future.

Money Trade Association: Resolves to Accommodate End-of-April Loan Extensions; Each Firm Decides on Flexibility Within Possible Scope; Implement Commercial Acceptance Bill Discounting; Banks Allocate Large Sums for Interbank Lending 118

Shanghai industrialists and merchants, concerned about the approaching end-of-April maturity dates for long-term loans, requested the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to ask the money trade for accommodations. The Money Trade Association held an executive committee meeting yesterday, and aside from notifying all firms in the trade, they principally approved the discounting of commercial acceptance bills. The Bankers Association has contacted the Central Bank to announce interest rates. Details are as follows:

Money Trade Association Executive Committee Meeting

The Money Trade Association held its 37th executive committee meeting of the second term at 2 PM yesterday at the association's meeting room on Ningbo Road. Attendees included Qin Runqing, Wang Huailian, Qian Yuansheng, Zheng Bingquan, Liu Wuqiao, Sheng Xiaoshan, Li Shoushan, and Zhang Mengzhou. Secretary-General Qin Xiqing was present as an observer. The meeting was chaired by Qin Runxiang, and after formal greetings, the following items were reported: (1) Minutes of the previous meeting; (2) Letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce forwarding the instruction from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau regarding the Central Political Conference resolution to protect people's property and business freedom; (3) Various reports on the reserve fund. Items for discussion included: (1) The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's letter regarding requests from factories and shops for accommodating methods for long-term notes nearing maturity, before the implementation of small-scale credit mortgages; (2) The Committee for Promoting National Goods' request to postpone fixed-term loans. A combined resolution was reached that each firm had already considered the situation and handled things as usual regarding long-term loans coming due, being repaid, extended, or newly issued, and a letter had been sent to notify all firms in the trade. (3) Regarding setting the date for the internal market conference, it was decided to be at 2 PM on April 25th. (4) Regarding commercial acceptance bill discounting, a principle approval was reached, and all firms in the trade would be notified to accept such instruments as much as possible for their regular business clients. The meeting adjourned around 3 PM.

Each Firm Decides on Maximum Flexibility

The money trade's long-term loans to industry and commerce were originally divided into three periods each year: end of March, end of September, and now end of April, end of October, each period being six months. With the end of April approaching, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, upon receiving requests from various industries, sent a letter to the Money Trade Association for accommodations. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency inquired with the money trade yesterday and learned that Article 29 of the trade's regulations states: "For fixed-term loans, debtors should repay on time. If the debtor wishes to repay before maturity, they must obtain the money shop's consent. However, if the money shop deems it necessary, it may also recover the loan from the debtor at any time with the debtor's consent, even before maturity." Now, each money shop has decided to provide flexibility for maturing loans within possible limits, in order to fulfill the purpose of supporting industry and commerce.

Banks Implement Bill Discounting

After the silk and satin trade association implemented commercial acceptance bills on April 1st, the Silk Industry Bank was the first to undertake discounting. After the Bankers Association passed six principles for implementation, it coordinated with the Central Bank to announce the discount rate daily while also handling rediscounting to facilitate the flow of funds between the banking and money trades. The Central Bank has largely resolved any issues with this approach, and all banks agree on the discounting principles as part of their business. Implementation will begin as soon as coordination is complete, resolved by the end of April.

Three Banks Exert Themselves to Relieve All Industries

With the end of April approaching, the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications have decided to set aside substantial funds, similar to the methods used before the industry account closures in 1934, for interbank lending between the banking and money trades, in order to indirectly relieve all industries. At the same time, the Bankers Association has raised 2.5 million yuan for small credit loans. If the government can allocate another 2.5 million yuan, totaling 5 million yuan, a bank syndicate will be organized to implement the plan. Otherwise, the banks will independently organize the syndicate. Implementation is resolved before the end of April to provide relief to industry and commerce. Detailed measures have been drafted and are being processed by a subcommittee.

First Preparatory Meeting for This Year's Cholera Prevention 121

At 3 PM on the 8th of this month, Director Liu Ruiheng of the National Health Administration convened a meeting for cholera prevention this year at the Shanghai Municipal Government. Attendees included Chairman Liu Ruiheng, Director Wu Liande of the Port Quarantine Administration, Director Li Tingan of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, Director Jordan of the Public Concession's Health Department, Director La Poudre of the French Concession's Health Department, G. Nanard of the Rockefeller Foundation's International Health Division, Section Chief Huang Zifang of the Jinpu Railway Bureau's Health Section, Deputy Director Jin Baoshan of the Central Health Experiment Bureau, Director Chen Zongxian of the Central Epidemic Prevention Bureau, Director Dunske of the Municipal Council's Chemical Laboratory, Chief Medical Officer Wu Changyao of the Port Quarantine Office (currently also serving as Secretary of the Provisional Office for Cholera Prevention), Consultant Chen Yonghan, Technician Borris, and Director Cheng Shuzhen of the Health Experiment Institute.

First, Director Li Tingan of the Municipal Health Bureau reported on the city's epidemic prevention situation last year, emphasizing the efforts in public education to ensure that all citizens paid attention to prevention and received vaccinations, along with the provision of free tap water, which greatly benefited the poor. As a result, no epidemic occurred last year. Next, the health authorities of the two concessions reported that the prevention results within the concessions last year were also good, with no epidemic. The methods used were still compulsory vaccination and the provision of free tap water to the poor, which proved most effective. Subsequently, Director Wu Liande of the Port Quarantine Administration, Director Cheng Shuzhen of the Health Experiment Institute, and Section Chief Huang Zifang of the two railway health sections each reported. Chairman Liu Ruiheng expressed satisfaction with the reports and hoped that efforts would continue this year to prevent an epidemic.

Next, committee members were assigned to each group: Epidemic Prevention Group: Wu Liande (Chairman), Dunske, La Poudre, Yan Fuqing, Luo Bu Sheng, Chen Yonghan, Yang Yongnian, Huang Zifang, Cheng Shuzhen. Publicity Group: Li Tingan (Chairman), Wu Changyao, La Poudre, Huang Zifang, Allen. It was decided that vaccinations would be earnestly implemented starting May 1st. A lengthy discussion followed regarding the vaccines and specific bacteria used, as well as the bacteria count. Cheng Shuzhen, Yang Yongnian, Jordan, and others all expressed opinions. Finally, Huang Zifang proposed, and Wu Liande seconded, the following decisions: (1) When possible, two injections should be given using a standard vaccine containing 2 billion bacteria, the first dose being half a cubic centimeter, and the second dose being one cubic centimeter. (2) If only one injection can be given, use the same vaccine with one cubic centimeter. (3) Inject a smaller number of people with a more concentrated vaccine, such as 4 billion and 8 billion bacteria, to observe its effectiveness and reactions. Regarding chemical testing, it was decided to implement a division of labor to avoid duplication. Fecal samples taken by the concessions would be tested by the Municipal Council's Chemical Laboratory, while fecal samples taken by the Chinese area would be tested by the Shanghai Municipal Health Experiment Institute. The total number of beds in the epidemic hospitals of both the Chinese and concession areas reached over a thousand. If a severe epidemic were to occur, temporary treatment centers would still need to be added. In Wusong, there is a newly built port quarantine hospital that can accommodate over 30 people. Regarding drinking water, it was decided to continue to find ways to provide free tap water so that the general poor population could avoid drinking river and pond sewage. Finally, the disinfection of well water was also fully discussed. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 PM.

Dangerous Hidden Reef Discovered in the Haitan Strait: Notification to Shipping Companies to Advise Vessels to Take Notice 122

The Minhai Customs' Haihe patrol vessel in the Haitan Strait of Fuzhou previously struck a reef and sank in that location. The vessel has not yet been salvaged. The Hydrographic Office of the Naval Department has found an extremely dangerous hidden reef 1,260 feet away from Niujiao Mountain in the Haitan Strait, at 129.5 degrees, approximately 4.72 nautical miles away, with a depth of only six feet below the sea surface. Its location is approximately at 119 degrees 40 minutes East longitude and 25 degrees 42 minutes North latitude, posing an extremely significant danger to the navigation of the Nan Hua Shipping Company's ships. An urgent notification is issued, ordering all companies to inform all seagoing vessels traveling to the ports of Min, Shantou, Xiamen, Quanzhou, and Xinghua to take special notice and to mark the dangerous hidden reef on nautical charts.

Director of the Shanghai Audit Office Talks: Audit Local Agencies First; The Office's Work Is Divided Into Three Categories 125

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Audit Office of the Audit Department was officially established in Shanghai on the 1st of this month. Director Lin Jinyu is currently contacting various parties and drafting various regulations to begin auditing work. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited Director Lin, and the discussion is as follows:

Three Types of Work

According to Director Lin, the office's work can be divided into three types: (1) Reviewing and signing payment orders and revenue orders; (2) Auditing calculations and final accounts; (3) Investigating acts of financial impropriety or dereliction of duty. This work is of great importance to finance, and the office will adhere to central laws and regulations and proceed earnestly. Various audit regulations and procedures are currently being drafted and will be started at the various agencies in the shortest possible time.

On-Site Auditing

The Audit Department originally required agencies to submit their accounts for auditing. Now, for the sake of solemnity and convenience, it has been changed to on-site auditing. The area under the office's jurisdiction is the Shanghai area, and all agencies established by the central and local governments must be audited on-site by the office.

Audit Steps

Agencies directly under the central government in Shanghai were originally audited by the Audit Department. At the beginning of the office's establishment, the agencies directly under the central government in Shanghai will be temporarily postponed from being transferred to the office's jurisdiction. However, local agencies have always been audited. After the office is established, it will first audit the accounts of local agencies. If it is successful, it will be extended to the agencies directly under the central government in Shanghai.

Coordination Completed

Since taking office, Director Lin has visited Mayor Wu Zhicheng twice. The office has sent personnel to contact Director Cai, and coordination has been completed. The office will send personnel to the municipal government within days for on-site auditing to avoid bureaucratic delays. In short, the audit office's audit work for various agencies will be done in the most straightforward way, so that the agencies will not be burdened with extra delays.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance to Request Exemption of Re-export Tax on Shandong Silk 126

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance yesterday: To the esteemed Finance Ministry in Nanjing, on the 9th of this month, we received a letter from the local silk and satin trade association stating: "We have received a letter from the Shandong and Henan silk group stating that our Shandong silk has always been transshipped through Yantai to Shanghai. During the prosperous period of Shandong silk's foreign trade in the late Qing Dynasty, Westerners from various foreign firms in Yantai organized a sericulture school. Due to lack of funds, they created a 'silk product levy,' collecting 4 taels of customs silver per dan as the school's recurring expenses. This levy was mandatory for all silk exporters, whether Chinese or foreign merchants. Later, as business declined and merchants could not bear the burden, there was widespread resistance. At that time, the Yantai Customs authorities, in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties, requested the government to exempt customs duties and only collect the silk product levy on all silk exported and transshipped. Since the government issued an order two years ago to exempt all silk exports from tax, the various foreign firms in Yantai collectively decided that since exports were exempt from tax, they were unwilling to continue paying the silk product levy and requested the customs to abolish it. After repeated negotiations, they actually achieved their goal, and the customs abolished the silk product levy and followed the new regulations. All goods exported to foreign countries and Hong Kong are tax-free. As a result, Western merchants can reduce costs by purchasing silk in Yantai due to the tax exemption, while our industry has to transship to Shanghai for sales to foreign firms, thereby increasing the burden of re-export tax. In this era of commercial warfare, with an atmosphere of immeasurable change pervading the globe, merchants who used to seek a profit of 10% are now struggling to secure 0.1%, which is not always guaranteed. Now, with the added burden of customs duties, which outsiders may consider minimal, the costs are different compared to the direct tax-free exports of Western merchants. Not only is it difficult to make a profit, but it will also be a major blow to future foreign trade. It was reported in the newspapers that Finance Minister Kong stated, 'Encouraging exports is the way to reduce trade deficits and ease the burden on the people. Therefore, I propose to the central government to separately reduce or exempt export taxes and abolish re-export taxes. However, reducing or exempting export taxes involves more categories and complex situations, making implementation slower. Abolishing re-export taxes is simple and easy to implement.' The members of our group, in light of the sluggish foreign trade and the re-export tax on goods shipped from Yantai to Shanghai, which prevents them from competing with the direct tax-free exports of Western merchants, have repeatedly suffered failures due to the different costs. The pain they have experienced for years is that goods shipped from Yantai to Shanghai are subject to re-export duties and half tax as well as pier dues. After arriving in Shanghai, due to various difficulties, they cannot be exported under the original permit, and merchants not only sacrifice customs duties but also have to pay pier dues again before they can export. With these kinds of hardships, it is difficult for them to compete with Western merchants and achieve victory. Now that Finance Minister Kong has shown concern for the people and compassion for the merchants, advocating to encourage exports and reduce the burden on the people, and proposing to the central government to separately reduce or exempt export taxes and abolish re-export taxes, it is a great relief to rescue merchants from fire and water. Therefore, we publicly agreed to request your association to forward the facts to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and present them to the Ministries of Finance and Industry for review and to consult the Customs Administration to order the Chief of Customs of the Jianghai Customs and the Customs Commissioner of Yantai to investigate and to order Western merchants to be allowed to immediately abolish the direct tax-free export from Yantai in order to alleviate the merchants' hardships. It is a matter of public convenience.' In light of the above, encouraging exports and reducing the burden on merchants is a matter of urgency. We respectfully request that your esteemed association show compassion for the merchants' hardships and quickly forward the facts separately, requesting a clear order to abolish the re-export tax on goods shipped from Yantai to Shanghai in order to relieve the people's plight and appease the public's expectations. This will be greatly appreciated." It has been heard that silk exports are tax-free, which has been implemented for many years. The government originally intended to promote foreign trade, but because Shandong Province is located inland and Chinese merchants do not have direct export trade, they still have to go through Western merchants in Shanghai. Therefore, this Shandong silk, in Yantai trade, is reported directly for export by Western merchants, while Chinese merchants still transship through Shanghai. Not only do they have to pay an additional re-export tax, but also pier dues in Shanghai. This is because of the tax on re-export and the absence of tax on export, so that the rights enjoyed by Western merchants are superior to those of Chinese merchants. At present, there has been much reporting on the re-export tax, although there is talk of complete abolition, implementation is still pending due to the issue of compensation. However, Shandong silk is a special case, and exports have long been tax-free. If the re-export tax is not abolished immediately, it will be difficult for Yantai Chinese merchants to compete with Western merchants who directly report for export. It is appropriate to cable your ministry, with the facts, requesting your approval to abolish the re-export tax immediately, in order to relieve the merchants' hardships, which is a matter of public convenience.

Due to the recent cloudy and rainy weather and rising tides in the Huangpu River, the Shanghai County Government has not completed the river projects dredged in the first, second, and third districts this year, including the Chaiwangjia Ditch, Huangni Bang, Tangchun Jing, Xin Gang, Sunjia Jing, Yaojia Bang Jing, and Dianni Bang. Therefore, County Magistrate Pan telegraphed the district heads yesterday to properly repair the dikes of each river to prevent them from collapsing, and to quickly drain the accumulated water to continue construction. If there are lawless people who try to be lazy in the project and open the dike privately, or if the contractors fail to drain the water, they should be reported separately, arrested, and sent to the county for investigation.

After the Yu Ji Mound is Dredged and the Dam is Built, the Inland River Traffic is Cut Off, and the Manure Boats Cannot Enter the Public Concession. The Public Concession Cleansing Department Has Taken Measures 134

The Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Committee, following the order of the National Economic Committee, dredged the Yu Ji Mound section of the Wusong River and simultaneously closed the dams at two locations near Beizhuang Jing and Yu Ji Mound Ye Jia Zhai on April 1st. After this, other ships, such as rice boats and barges, can still detour through the Nan Gong Pu to enter the Wusong River. However, manure boats are small and light and cannot navigate the Gong Pu, causing a great panic in Shanghai's manure export. It has been reported that the Fuchang Company Cleansing Bureau, affiliated with the Public Concession Public Works Department, has leased a large number of large and small boats since April 1st to transport manure from the entire concession to Pudong and Beixin Jing, where they are buried in pits, so there is no problem. However, the company has suffered huge losses due to the cessation of business and the need to invest in leasing ships for transportation. It is said that the Zhabei District Cleansing Department will also take similar measures.

Ships Switch to Metric Ton System, Ministry of Communications Supplements Implementation Measures, to be Implemented on May 1st, Order Issued to Navigation Administration Bureau Yesterday 135

The Ministry of Communications originally planned to implement the metric ton system for ships under the Maritime Commerce Law on April 1st, but due to insufficient preparation, it was postponed to May 1st. It is reported that the Ministry of Communications believed that the metric ton system proposed earlier still needed to be supplemented, so the Ministry of Communications yesterday instructed the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau, "The case of changing ships to the metric ton system under the Maritime Commerce Law, we have approved the National Bureau of Weights and Measures' six unified principles of navigation administration weights and measures, which have been ordered to be followed in our instruction No. 652 on February 2nd. Now, according to the reports from various bureaus and offices, opinions on the implementation of the reform have been received by the Ministry, and after detailed compilation and verification by the Ministry, eleven supplementary measures and three forms have been formulated. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued to the bureau to strictly abide by and implement it."
