Chongming County Business Tax Collection Office Levies Temporary Business Tax on the Fishing Industry, Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association Believes it Violates the Ban and Writes to the Government Requesting Prompt Revocation 138

The Shengshan Islands, affiliated with the fifth district of Chongming County, are fishing areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. Every time the fishing season arrives, fishermen and fish merchants from various gangs gather, most of whom are from Zhejiang, such as the former Taizhou and Wenzhou areas, but the most are from Ningbo. It is reported that the Chongming County Business Tax Collection Office has set up a collection branch in the area, levied a temporary business tax on the fishing industry, and ordered the brokers to collect 0.5% of the value of the goods sold by the merchants as business tax. The fishermen and fish merchants in the area were shocked when they heard the news and reported it to the Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association in Shanghai, requesting assistance. The association believes that the government has already issued orders to abolish fish tax and fishing tax. The collection office is cleverly establishing a new name to engage in collection, which is a great loss to the central government's intention to protect the fishing industry. The association will appeal to the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting an order to stop it. The document states, "According to reports from Ningbo fishermen and fish merchants, the Chongming County Business Tax Collection Office has posted a notice to levy a temporary business tax on the fishing industry on the islands affiliated with the fifth district of Chongming. A collection branch has been established in the fifth district to prepare for the collection of business tax in the district. The brokers are ordered to collect 0.5% of the value of the goods sold by the merchants as a temporary business tax on the fishing industry. The fishermen and fish merchants were shocked when they heard the news. It has been found that the fishing industry has been declining recently, and the government, in order to maintain the fishing industry, ordered the abolition of the Fisheries Department and prohibited the collection of taxes under new names in the future, and has repeatedly emphasized this. Now, the collection office is collecting a temporary fish business tax similar to the fish tax, which is a contempt for the ban. The fishermen and fish merchants are unable to bear it. Please make an appeal, etc. It has been found that since foreign aggression, China's fishing industry has been in danger. In 1931, the government, in order to protect the fishing industry, issued an order to abolish fish tax and fishing tax and prohibited the collection of disguised fish taxes to relieve the people's difficulties. Now, the collection office is cleverly establishing a new name to engage in collection, which is a great loss to the central government's intention to protect the fishing industry. According to the previous situation, we should send a letter for review, order the cessation of collection to maintain the fishing industry, and relieve the people's difficulties."

Robbery Case at French Water and Electricity Company: Seven Unrelated Persons Released First 139

On February 20th of this year, at around 10 AM, at the French Water and Electricity Company at 249 Luban Road, the compradore Tu Jinming was taking cash of 20,000 yuan to the bank for storage when he was suddenly attacked by four robbers outside the company's gate. 4,000 yuan was robbed and they fled. The case was investigated by Jin Jiulin, the director of the special agency of the French patrol room, and the patrol officers on duty, who successively arrested Zhang Deji, Pan Yibang, Zhang Yunpeng, Fan Youheng, Xu Xiaogen, Zhu Hanqiang, Pan Yuqing, Yang Yang, Li Zhongxin, Liu Shaogen, Zhao Zhongheng, Xing Yanshou, Zhou Kui, Zhou Lu, Xia Wenfu, Xu Yuecheng, Xu Defu and other 17 men and women suspected of being involved in the robbery and seized handguns and bullets. The arrestees were sent to the Second Special District Local Court requesting detention pending detailed investigation, as reported three times previously. The patrol room has concluded its investigation and sent the defendants to the court for interrogation yesterday morning. At 10 AM, Judge Sun Pengxian and clerk Tao Zongkan went to the criminal court to conduct the interrogation. Attorney Fei Xizhen, representing the police department, stated that it was found that the defendants Zhang De, Fan Youheng, Yang Yang, Liu Shaogen, Zhao Zhongheng, Qiu Yanshou, Zhou Kui, Zhou Lu, and Xu Defu were involved in the robbery. Yang Yang and the fugitive Wang Houqi colluded with the defendants in the case to rob the French Water and Electricity Company of 4,000 yuan, and Yang Yang opened fire. Fortunately, no one was injured. Afterwards, he received 500 yuan for spending and lent the handgun to others for robbery. Although the ninth defendant, Xu Defu, was not involved in the French Water and Electricity Company robbery, he committed another robbery. He is now being prosecuted for robbery with a deadly weapon by a group of three or more people under Article 348 of the Criminal Law. The patrol room found no evidence of crimes committed by Pan Yibang, Zhang Yunpeng, Xu Shaogen, Zhu Hanqiang, Pan Yuqing, Li Zhongxin, Xia Wenfu, and Xu Yuecheng, and they will not be prosecuted. Except for Pan Yibang, who committed a crime in the interior and the Water Police team requested temporary detention, the others should be released. Attorney Ba He, representing the plaintiff, the French Water and Electricity Company, stated that the plaintiff requests a private prosecution to recover the stolen 4,000 yuan. The court checked the report and, considering the complexity of the case and that it was almost noon, ordered that the interrogation be postponed to the 19th. Zhang Yunpeng, Xu Shaogen, Zhu Hanqiang, Pan Yuqing, Li Zhongxin, Xia Wenfu, and Xu Yuecheng were not prosecuted by the patrol room and should be released. The remaining defendants were returned to custody pending further instructions.

Ignorant of Suicide as a Sin, Young Passenger Throws Himself into the Sea; Suicide by Throwing Himself into the Sea off the Outer Tongsha Sea Area with Two Letters and Two Photographs, Marriage Planned for this Winter, Cause of Death Unknown 140

The Xinhongxing ship, owned by the Daxing Shipping Company on the Bund, Shanghai, departed from Shanghai for Ningbo at 5 PM on the 8th. When the ship was passing the outer Tongsha Sea area, a young passenger committed suicide by throwing himself into the sea. The facts are as follows:

Sudden Disappearance

The Xinhongxing ship set sail from the Daxing Wharf on the Bund at 5 PM on the 8th and departed for Ningbo. At around 12 AM that night, when the ship was passing the Outer Tongsha, near the Daji Sea, Zhao Delin, the steward of compartment 106 in the steerage, noticed that a young passenger in the adjacent berth had not returned to his berth. It was late at night, and all the windows were closed, so there was no reason for him to be loitering outside the compartment. He searched but found no trace of him.

Letters Discovered

Later, two letters and two photographs were found in his berth. There were no other belongings. At this point, it was known that he had committed suicide by throwing himself into the river. The steward examined the letters, photographs, and other items and reported them to the accounting room. After reading the letters, it was learned that the deceased's name was Zhou Shigui, 19 years old, from Fengshi Town, Yinxi, Ningbo. One of the letters was addressed to his cousin Wang Wenhe, and the address on the letter was Rongtai Cotton Cloth Shop, 10 Jifu Lane, Ningbo Road. The other letter was addressed to his parents.

Not Yet Married

One of the two photographs was of a middle-aged woman, and the other was said to be of his friend. The above letters and photographs were sent by the steward Zhao Delin to Rongchang Cotton Cloth Shop on Ningbo Road, the residence of his cousin Wang Wenhe, after the ship returned to Shanghai from Ningbo yesterday. According to the reporter's inquiry from the second compradore Yu Tinglai of the ship and Rongchang Shop, the cause of death is unknown. It is only known that the deceased was scheduled to marry this winter. His family has been notified by telegram from his cousin Wang Wenhe (the owner of Rongchang Shop).

Two Letters

(1) Respectfully to my dear parents: I am writing to inform you that, due to various sufferings, I have no heart to live. I have achieved my goal today. I hope you will not be sad or commemorate me. Take care of yourselves. I will not say more. Please comfort yourselves. Wishing you happiness. (2) Cousin Wenhe: I hope you are well and everything is fine. I miss you very much. I am writing to you for nothing else. I have unspeakable pain in my heart and have no choice but to end my life in the sea tonight. If there is any emergency in my family, please take care of it. I entrust this to you a thousand times. I will repay you in the next life. Please forgive me. Goodbye, Wenhe.

Not Awakened Until Death

On the newspaper used to wrap the photographs, the following words were written in pencil, which seemed to be left in the last moment before death. It can be said that he was not awakened until death: "So sad, dying in the sea, my body being swallowed by a big fish. It really saves money, no coffin, no money. It is really satisfying to die like this."

Port Authority Dredges New Channel in Huangpu River; Buoys to be Removed at the End of This Week 141

According to Datong News Agency, the new channel in the Huangpu River, which is located opposite Gaoqiao Sand, between Zhanghuabang, has been open for some time. Since the channel was opened, it has become a necessary route for ships entering and leaving the Huangpu River. The old channel (slightly to the east) has long been abandoned. Later, the Port Authority, considering that the number of imported ships has been increasing, felt that the channel needed to be widened and dredged further. The Port Authority Director Gu Lien, in consultation with the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau, started dredging on December 1st of last year. Since the project was actively dredged by the No. 2 Hailong Dredging Ship dispatched by the Chief Engineer of the Dredging Bureau and other personnel, it has been more than four months. The entire project has now been completed. In terms of engineering, the east and west ends have been widened by 300 feet each (a total of 600 feet). The length is divided into two locations, one for 3.5 kilometers and one for 1.5 kilometers. The completion of this project will naturally make ships entering and leaving the Huangpu River feel more comfortable. The marker ships set up by the Customs to guide the ships can also be removed by the end of this week.

In order to revitalize industry and promote the development of international trade, the Central Bank plans to build Qiujiang Wharf warehouses and operate and build industrial areas related to the wharf. It is reported that the land has been circled according to the list of civilian land requisitioned by the Municipal Land Bureau. All designs have also been completed. The bank issued a notice yesterday inviting merchants to bid for construction, and it is scheduled to open the bids publicly in the Central Bank's third-floor parlor at 10 AM on May 10th. Construction can begin as soon as bidders are found.

Large Dredging Ship of the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau Passed Singapore Yesterday; Smith Returned to Shanghai to Report on the Manufacturing Process; Sounding of the Tiaohe Shoal Completed, Dredging to Begin in Early Next Month; Arrival in Shanghai Around the 20th of This Month 143

The Huangpu River Dredging Bureau specially ordered the largest dredging ship from Germany to dredge the Tiaohe Shoal at the mouth of the Yangtze River. It has already set sail for China and passed Singapore yesterday. The supervisor Smith has returned to Shanghai to report on the construction process. The dredging work will begin in early next month. The details are as follows:

Dredging Ship has Arrived in Singapore

The Huangpu River Dredging Bureau ordered the largest dredging ship "Jianshe" from the German Xuegao Shipyard two years ago, costing 2.5 million yuan, for the purpose of dredging the Tiaohe Shoal in the Yangtze River. After the ship was completed, it set sail for China at the beginning of last month. Due to the heavy equipment and the bluntness of the hull, the voyage was slow. Yesterday morning, the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau telegraphed Singapore to inquire about the situation of the ship. According to the telegram, it had just passed through and docked the night before and had already set sail for Shanghai. It is estimated that the voyage from Singapore to Shanghai will take at the latest around the 20th of this month.

Supervisor Smith Returned to Shanghai

When the German Xuegao Company contracted to build the dredging ship, the Bureau specially sent engineer Smith, a Westerner, and Zhu Chongxi, to Germany two years ago to supervise the construction. Now that the ship has been completed, supervisor Smith returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday to report everything to the Bureau. Engineer Zhu Chongxi is now accompanying the ship to Shanghai.

Dredging of Tiaohe Shoal to Begin Next Month

The sounding work of the Tiaohe Shoal outside Wusong was completed by the Hydrographic Office of the Naval Department. The location of the shoal is between Tongsha and Guansha in the Yangtze River. There are detailed reports on its area, orientation, and the amount of sediment. According to engineer Ge Tuo of the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau yesterday, after the dredging ship arrives in Shanghai, the inspection and acceptance procedures will be carried out first, and the dredging of the shoal will begin at the beginning of next month, with approximately 20,000 cubic meters of mud being dredged daily. After the dredging, navigation can be guaranteed to be unimpeded.

Confrontation with Robbers Resulting in Death; Looted Goods Found on the Deceased, Seven Bullets Wounds, None Penetrated 144

At around 6 AM the day before yesterday, three robbers broke into the home of Dr. Wang Shiting at No. 16 Yuanchang Lane, Yuanchang Road, Hongkou, each armed with a handgun, and demanded silence. They robbed silver and jewelry, totaling more than 100 yuan. As the robbers were about to escape, Wang followed them and informed the patrol officers, who jointly pursued them, resulting in a gun battle. As a result, one robber was arrested, seriously wounded by gunfire. He was sent to the patrol hospital, but died before medical assistance could be given. A Westerner was killed by a stray bullet, and several passersby were injured. The details have been reported in this newspaper. The Hongkou Patrol Room dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. The body of the robber was taken to the Philan Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Local Court sent prosecutor Guo Wei, forensic doctor Wei, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others to the morgue to examine the body. The Western patrol chief Kang Ming reported on the investigation and stated that the stolen gold and silver jewelry and a handgun with five bullets were found on the deceased. He is currently investigating and tracking down the escaped robbers. Wang Shiting, 34 years old, from Dongtai, a doctor, reported that at around 6 AM yesterday morning, three robbers, each armed with a handgun, entered through the back door, all with local accents. They ordered me to take out the safe, but I replied that there was no such safe. Therefore, they robbed approximately 30 to 40 yuan in banknotes and silver, gold and silver jewelry, and left. Afterwards, I followed them and informed the patrol officers, and identified the deceased as one of the three robbers. After hearing the report, prosecutor Guo Wei determined that the deceased was an unnamed man who resisted arrest and was shot and killed by the police on the spot. The bullets in the body should be removed by the forensic doctor and handed over to the patrol room's gun identification department. The handgun and bullets found on the deceased were also handed over to the gun identification department for inspection. The escaped robbers will be arrested and prosecuted by the patrol room. The body was handed over to Pushan Villa for burial. It was also learned that the deceased had seven gunshot wounds, and the bullets did not penetrate. Forensic doctor Wei is currently trying to remove them.

An Englishman Sues Zhou Bingshen for Land Fraud: A Deed Transferred Under a Proxy Name Changed to the Principal's Name 147

Zhou Bingshen, a Ningbo native and former manager of the Three Stars Stage, previously served as a comprador for the British-owned "Tide Surge" Water Company. He later ventured into real estate, co-founding the Three Stars Real Estate Company with Huang Chujiu, Zhao Ruquan, and others. Due to business failures, Zhou sold the Three Stars Stage, leading to numerous lawsuits. Zhou has now moved his family to Shaoxing.

An Englishman named Lai Wuzhe, an accountant for the British-owned water company, entrusted Zhou on December 29, 1931, to purchase land and buildings at 397 and 398 Qipu Road, for a price of 5,777 taels of silver. Lai paid with a check and, upon receiving the deed, asked Zhou to obtain the land ownership certificate from the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau. Zhou repeatedly delayed the process, citing the need for "fees." Recently, Lai discovered that Zhou had indeed obtained the land ownership certificate from the Land Bureau, but the certificate was issued in Zhou Bingshen's name. Furthermore, on August 19, 1933, Zhou mortgaged the land certificate to the Jiangnan Bank for 12,000 yuan. Lai believes Zhou Bingshen's actions constitute fraud and reported the matter to the Public Concession Police Headquarters.

Following investigations by Chinese Detective Feng Zhiming and a Western detective, an arrest warrant was requested from the First Special District Court and served at 12 Anyi Lane, Wuding Road. However, Zhou had already relocated to Shaoxing. The warrant was then delivered to Zhou's civil case lawyer. Yesterday morning, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court held a criminal hearing. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu presented the case, charging Zhou with fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Code and submitting the check as evidence. Zhou's civil litigation lawyer appeared in court, stating that Zhou had moved to Shaoxing and that the exact address would need to be verified and reported later, requesting the court to formally request assistance from the Shaoxing court for the summons. Lawyer Zhang immediately requested that if Zhou's address could not be verified, a warrant for his arrest should be issued. The presiding judge reviewed the request and ordered the case adjourned for two weeks.

Foreign Cigarette Merchants Increase Sales by Over 30,000 Cases per Month, Chinese Merchants Hit Hard 150

A reporter from the Shang Guo Wen She (Business News Agency) met with Mr. Shen Weiting, chairman of the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Merchants Association, who stated that in recent months, the sales of foreign cigarettes have increased significantly, by approximately 36,000 cases per month compared to the past. The reasons are twofold: (1) Foreign cigarette merchants are dumping cigarettes at low prices. For example, the "Little Fairy" brand used to sell for over 160 yuan per case, but now it has dropped to 142 yuan per case, and each empty pack can be exchanged for one cigarette. Each case contains 5,000 packs, which can be exchanged for 5,000 cigarettes, worth approximately 14 yuan. The actual selling price per case is 128 yuan. The cost of raw materials and labor is approximately 30 yuan, and taxes are 80 yuan. After adding discounts and commissions, there is little profit left. Chinese merchants cannot afford to compete. However, foreign merchants have strong capital and are not currently focused on making money, but on defeating Chinese merchants in order to monopolize the market permanently. (2) In the past, Chinese cigarette factories could still use gifts to promote their products, which attracted more customers, even with limited resources and methods. However, since the ban on gifts, Chinese merchants have lost their promotional tools. Coupled with the pressure of foreign merchants dumping, the future is very dangerous.

The "Linxing" ship, which sank in the Yangtze River channel outside the Wusong Estuary, 323 degrees from the Ninth Section Lighthouse, 2 nautical miles away, at 121 degrees 38 minutes East longitude and 31 degrees 21 minutes North latitude, as previously reported in detail, has been salvaged. Establishment of the Shanghai Alumni Association of the National Police Academy 163

The National Police Academy, founded by the former Ministry of Internal Affairs in 1917, has graduated more than ten classes. All graduates were submitted to the ministry and assigned to various provinces for employment. After completing a one-year internship in the province, they were employed as recommended police officers. Therefore, the police organs in various provinces are led by graduates of the Police Academy. After the national capital was established in Nanjing, the Ministry of Internal Affairs moved the Beijing Police Academy to Nanjing. At the same time, Police Academy alumni serving in the police force of the capital established the Police Academy Alumni Association. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau also employs dozens of Police Academy graduates. Therefore, on the 23rd of last month, the founding meeting of the Shanghai Alumni Association of the National Police Academy was held at the People's Education Center in the Wenmiao Temple in Nanshi. Five directors, three supervisors, and various staff members were elected in accordance with the regulations to actively carry out association affairs. Representatives from the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau were sent to provide guidance, and the order was very good. The association then issued a declaration informing Police Academy alumni across the country to unite and initiate actions in their respective regions to achieve the goal of revitalizing the national police administration and creating a new country. The text of the declaration is as follows: "The people of the country have suffered from disturbances for a long time. The lack of stability in the localities and the lack of order lead to the inability to live in peace and the inability to work happily. As a result, scholars are noisy in schools, farmers are lazy in the fields, and industry and commerce are exhausted in the markets. Those who observe the country say that this is a disease of the country's police administration. However, our country has been nurturing police talents for many years. Because the nurturing of ordinary police talents is insufficient, we are nurturing higher-level police talents to enable them to use what they have learned to perform their duties, so that the police administration will become increasingly enlightened. Those who know say that this is not because the higher-level police talents are incapable, but because the higher-level police talents have not fully demonstrated their abilities. The country has established the Police Academy for eighteen years. It is governed by a special ministry and defined by special subjects. From 1917 to the present, they have continued to graduate, assign, and employ, from the central government to various provinces, without counting the thousands of people, accounting for a small half of the statistics of police officials across the country. However, the police chiefs of various provinces, who are filled by higher-level police talents, are still not numerous. In modern times, military affairs are related to the police, and it is said that the police and law and politics are connected. In various countries in the East and West, police officers are specialized officials and cannot be compared with each other. Although, there is no need to worry, now the Ministry of Internal Affairs is moving the Police Academy to the capital, and personally and carefully training them. This shows that they value the role of higher-level police talents. Then we are fortunate to be in Shanghai, the center of politics, culture, and economy, where we can easily adapt and make achievements. If we do not take this opportunity to combine our wisdom and gather our strength, to contribute to the improvement of the police administration and to study the advancement of police science, would we not be betraying the grand heart of valuing higher-level police talents? The members of the Shanghai Alumni Association of the National Police Academy have been established. We hereby reveal this righteousness and tell the students in various provinces and cities that promoting a new life, creating a new life, and creating a new country must begin with revitalizing the national police administration. My fellow students, let us come together."

Then, the judge ordered the lawyers of both sides to argue, and then announced the conclusion of the case, scheduling the sentencing for the 15th.

Chen Jinlan, a Ningbo native nicknamed "Snake Skin Jinlan," was arrested by the French police and sent to the Second Special Court for shooting and killing Chen Zhikui, the owner of the Qianfengtai Candle Shop at 52 Dongxinqiao Street, French Concession, on the afternoon of April 14, 1933. As previously reported, the trial has been concluded. Yesterday, Judge Zhang and Prosecutor Wang held a special criminal hearing in the Second Court and ordered Fang and Zhou to be brought to the court. Fang Yuqi was sentenced to two years and six months imprisonment, and Zhou Wenjin was sentenced to two years imprisonment. The Four Banks Joint Treasury Issues Reserve Report, No. 275 171

The Four Banks Joint Treasury, jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Continental Banks, specializes in issuing Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guarantee reserves accounting for at most 40%. A public announcement is made every week, audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 275th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Treasury for April 6, Year 24, is transcribed below: Banknotes in circulation: 23,100,9473 yuan. Total reserves: 23,100,9473 yuan, including Cash reserves: 16,994,073 yuan. Guarantee reserves: 6,115,400 yuan.

China New Village Construction Company Proposes: Reforming the Real Estate Investment System; Advocating a New Model of Cooperative Investment in New Village Real Estate, Opening Up a New Avenue for Real Estate Investors 175

Due to the decline of the rural economy within the city and the impact of the global recession from abroad, credit contraction has led to currency tightening, causing real estate to stagnate. Taking real estate as an example, financial institutions mostly refuse mortgages, and vacant houses are everywhere. Those who have already invested are troubled by interest payments, and those who wish to invest are wary of repeating past mistakes. As a result, the real estate market in this city has fallen into stagnation. This phenomenon is partly due to the impact of the economic recession, but the poor investment system is the main cause. Unreasonable management and a lack of meticulous planning, even with abundant funds, are like throwing money into a bottomless pit. In view of this, the China New Village Construction Company, based on the principle of savings and adopting a cooperative method, has created a new model of cooperative investment in new village real estate. This method involves investors depositing their funds into the bank designated by the company. The company then builds the houses designated by the residents in the new village. After completion and handover, the investors collect rent and interest. This method, due to the balance of supply and demand, eliminates the risk of vacant rentals and provides reliable profits. The company's operating policy is based on building new villages and connecting to the spirit of rural prosperity, progressing gradually according to its own capabilities, solving housing problems for urban residents on the one hand and opening up a bright path for investors on the other. The specific measures for cooperative investment in new village real estate have been planned and will be announced soon. Details are recorded below:

Hiring of Consultants

The cooperative investment method for new village real estate created by the company extracts the strengths of general real estate investment and corrects its shortcomings, creating a new and rational real estate investment system. The company, in establishing this method, is still in its early stages, and it is closely related to the future of the business. Therefore, it attaches great importance to it. In addition to inviting many experts to carefully study and formulate the method, it has also hired Zhang Naiqi, Li Quanshi, Pan Xulun, and Zhu Gengxin as consultants. These four are economists who serve in the financial sector. At the same time, an agency department has been added to handle real estate investment matters. It is said that Mr. Sun Dingcheng has been hired as the director of the department. Mr. Sun graduated from Jinling University and has served as a foreign secretary at the Jianghan Customs, a director of the Dalian Customs Special Photography Station, and a director of accounting at the Tianjin Customs. He has extensive knowledge and experience.

Eight Major Advantages

The cooperative real estate investment method created by the company examines the shortcomings of current businesses and corrects them, so it has the following advantages: (1) No limitation on capital. Based on the principle of cooperation, only funds of 500 yuan or more are required to invest in this real estate business. (2) Remedy for the ills of vacant rentals. According to the principle of balancing supply and demand, houses are built only after there are residents, ensuring that there are absolutely no vacant rentals. (3) Increase the interest rate on real estate investment. After the investment funds are handed over to the bank for collection, interest will accrue from the second day onwards, without any loss of interest during the intermediate period. (4) Reduce all due expenses. Investing in this real estate can reduce all due expenses, such as management fees, repair fees, and land taxes and housing depreciation. (5) Solid and Surpassing Guarantee. All the real estate invested by the investor provides an individual guarantee, and the original value is reduced by 10%. Only 90% of the cost is required to enjoy 100% of the rights. (6) Avoid Difficulties in Transfer. This real estate investment method has a fixed term and guarantees no vacant rentals, making it extremely easy to transfer. (7) Eliminate Troublesome Procedures. Investing in this real estate eliminates extremely troublesome matters, such as selecting locations, managing neighborhoods, planning rentals, and dealing with tenants. (8) No need to possess real estate investment knowledge. The company employs professionals to handle all matters, and they are well aware of the advantages and disadvantages of real estate. Investors can rest assured.

Collecting Bank

The China Economic Credit Cooperative Fund Management Committee, which manages the company's investment funds, has entrusted the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to collect funds in order to facilitate investors. Anyone wishing to make a cooperative real estate investment with the company can go to the company to fill out an investment trust form, sign the trust, and leave a seal impression at the company. At the same time, they can collect a payment notice and pay the total amount of the entrusted investment to the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications. They can then exchange the receipt for a New Village Real Estate Cooperative Investment Certificate of the same amount from the company. The total amount of the company's first phase of cooperative real estate investment is temporarily set at 500,000 yuan, and solicitation will continue until the full amount is reached.

Zhang Yongnian Talks

According to Mr. Zhang Yongnian, general manager of the company, if we want to seek the development of Shanghai, we must first engage in the revitalization of the rural economy. To make a tree grow tall, we must strengthen its roots. The purpose of establishing the New Village business is based on this idea. With the support of various sectors, the Rose Garden New Village is progressing smoothly and is now actively under construction. Completion is expected soon. The advocacy of cooperative investment in new village real estate opens up a bright path for real estate investors and expands the scope of the Rose Garden New Village. It is hoped that all sectors will actively invest to promote a prosperous rural society.

Jin Cheng Bank 1934 Business Report (28) 179

(8) Conclusion: Banks have a mission in the national economy. Therefore, their business policies should be based on observing and assessing economic trends and properly assisting their development in order to fulfill their responsibilities. The domestic and international economic situation and various developments in the bank's business in 1934 have been briefly outlined above. However, we must examine the past and assess the future to determine the future direction of the Chinese and foreign economies and to serve as a basis for the bank's policies. The economic relationship between the major countries of the world and our country is most significant in terms of trade and foreign exchange, especially the United States, Britain, and Japan, which are at the forefront of our trade. The trade balance of these three countries has shown good results due to currency inflation and exchange dumping. In the near future, their policies are unlikely to change drastically. Although European countries such as France and Italy still maintain the gold standard, their trade relations should also restrict imports and encourage exports by appropriate means. The second Five-Year Plan is also nearing completion, and the dumping of low-grade industrial products and agricultural products may become even more severe. Moreover, countries, based on their group economic policies, collect low-priced raw materials, promote their products, and strive to expand their groups in order to extend their influence. Our country is in a special position and has long been watched by the great powers. In particular, if the United States' national silver policy does not change, the economic circles of our country may continue to be affected. However, adversity can strengthen the country. If the government and all sectors of society can fulfill their responsibilities and work together, it will not be difficult to cope. According to the government authorities, the "procedures should be determined and implemented successively according to the current situation of the national economy and its possible development." Regarding the rumored currency inflation policy, it is also said that "it is absolutely not suitable for China and will harm the interests of the entire people. The government has no intention of adopting it." Therefore, the principles of economic construction and monetary policy of our government in the future have been announced. However, how to promote domestic basic industries, daily necessities industries, and important agricultural and mineral products to revitalize industries and achieve self-sufficiency, how to limit the large-scale import of agricultural products, food, and certain industrial products, and encourage their export to prevent leakage and seek a balance of trade, as well as improve international payment relations, and how to adjust foreign exchange and improve currency, it is expected that the government will be able to coordinate the overall situation and set specific plans as early as possible and implement them effectively. Among them, restricting the import of agricultural products and promoting domestic production are closely related to the revival of rural areas. Since the government presides over and promotes it, the society should support its implementation. However, even in terms of the rural economy, its scope is broad, and its organization is not yet complete. The contribution of our financial industry is not easy. It seems appropriate to concentrate our efforts and work together to achieve the effect of mutual support. As for this bank, which is a commercial bank, it is limited in its ability, but it will do its best to provide services. In addition to working together with all sectors of society and the industry, it will continue to work hard to achieve what it can do. The following are the respective measures: (1) In terms of credit, this bank is fortunate to be recognized by society and entrusted with funds. In the future, it should strive for the proper and convenient accumulation of funds, the prudent use of funds, and the joint reduction of deposit interest rates with the industry to reduce the capital cost of social undertakings and promote their development. (2) In terms of lending, this bank, in its position as a commercial bank, should provide assistance to various businesses in accordance with the principles of commercial finance. All investments should avoid non-production. Therefore, it has always provided assistance to production undertakings, and it is particularly willing to assist in the circulation of its products. It should continue to work with all sectors of society and the industry to assist in rural economy, mining and chemical industries, daily necessities industries, and railway transportation. As for important agricultural products such as food and cotton, and large-scale mineral products such as coal, jointly or independently, conduct various research and improvements in production and marketing, provide the use of appropriate institutions, and facilitate financing. It should also continue to cooperate with local authorities to support the sound development of small-scale agricultural, industrial, and commercial businesses. Warehouses are of great benefit to the circulation of goods and the turnover of industrial capital. In addition to having goods machines in major commercial ports and some rural areas, this bank should also consider setting up warehouses along railway lines to facilitate the distribution of products. (3) In terms of personnel, this bank is increasing its services to all sectors of society, so it feels it is necessary to cultivate appropriate talents. In the future, the policy of employing people should still be based on examination and training, so that they can be used according to their abilities. In short, this bank's business should continue to carefully examine the economic environment from time to time, and it should still be based on the consistent principle of prudent development, and it should work harder to make a small contribution to the national economy, so as to live up to the kindness of our shareholders and those in society who care for this bank. We hope that our shareholders and people from all walks of life will not hesitate to encourage and guide us, so that we can make more contributions. We look forward to it.

Sports News

The Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee Meeting Concluded Yesterday; Regulations for Sports Fields Submitted in Writing to the Ministry of Education for Approval; Sports Goods Exhibition Handed Over to the All-China Games Preparatory Committee 181

The Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee continued its meeting at the Jiaotong University Gymnasium at 9:00 AM yesterday, discussing several important proposals, and concluded at 1:00 PM in the afternoon, bringing the meeting to a close. The details are as follows:

Attendees: Yesterday's attendees included the following members of the Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee: Hao Gengsheng, Wu Yunrui, Ma John, Yuan Jiaoli, Cheng Dengke, Wu Ji, Zhang Huilan, Zhang Xinli, Ma Liang, and the directors of sports fields from various provinces and cities: Wu Bangwei from Jiangsu, Xu Yongxiang from Jiangxi, Zhang Zhongfan from Nanjing, Wang Zhuangfei from Shanghai (representing Xiang Xianggao), Zhu Jiasheng from Zhejiang, Xu Minhui from Guangdong, Zhang Yixian from Qingdao, Huang Fengqi from Changsha, Gu Yuqi from Henan, Shang Shumei from Shandong, Zhao Wenzao from Tianjin, Ke Nanshan from Wuchang, and more than twenty others. Hao Gengsheng served as chairman, Shao Rugan as secretary, and Zhang Boling and Zhang Jiong traveled to Beijing the night before.

Director's Report: After the formal opening ceremony, Chairman Hao Gengsheng stood up and stated that at this meeting, except for representatives from Yunnan, Sichuan, and Guizhou, who were absent due to the long journey, and Wang Shulan from Anhui, who was unable to attend due to illness, all the directors of sports fields from various provinces and cities were gathered to express their insightful opinions, which was fortunate for the sports community. Then, Zhang Zhongfan, the director of the Nanjing Sports Field, reported that Wang Shulan, the director of the Anhui Sports Field, had already started his journey to Shanghai to attend the meeting but suffered from severe diarrhea when passing through Nanjing and had to turn back midway, entrusting him to make a brief report on his behalf, as follows: The annual recurring expenses of the Anhui Sports Field are 10,248 yuan. In terms of organization, it is divided into two departments: guidance and administration, with a total of four staff members. Due to the inconvenient transportation and closed-mindedness of the people in Anhui Province, there are two sports fields in the provincial capital, one inside the province and one outside the city. Since July of the 20th year of the Republic, significant progress has been made in the past three years. In the past, there were disagreements and disputes in the joint sports meetings of primary and secondary schools, but such incidents no longer occur.

Discussion of Regulations: The discussion then began on: (1) the draft regulations for sports fields. It was resolved to submit the following matters to the Ministry of Education for review: A. The name should be prefixed with the name of the location, such as Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Sports Field (and so on). B. The organization should still follow the original proposal for departmental division. C. The minimum standards for the area and equipment of sports fields at all levels will be determined and included in the regulations after investigation by the Ministry of Education. D. The director and staff should be full-time in principle. E. The director may also serve as the head of a department but may not receive additional salary. F. In Article 9 of the draft regulations, the word "field residence" should be changed to "position". G. Contingency expenses should also be included. H. The minimum expenditure limit for provincial sports fields should also be stipulated. It was also decided that the regulations should be reported in writing by the directors of each field, and submitted to the Ministry of Education by the end of May. The report content should be divided into: A. Objectives, B. Organization, C. Expenses, D. Field and equipment, E. Work policy, F. Future plans, G. Special work and progress.

Exhibition of Supplies: (2) Committee member Hao Gengsheng proposed that physical education be included in the high school entrance examination curriculum. It was resolved to request the Ministry of Education to promptly issue measures for the physical education subject in the high school graduation examination. Before the issuance, each province and city may conduct spot checks as appropriate. (3) Committee member Cheng Dengke proposed that a national sports goods exhibition should be held. It was resolved to hand it over to the preparatory committee of the 6th All-China Games. (4) Committee member Cheng Dengke proposed that a national sports achievement exhibition hall should be established. It was resolved that the committee should request the Ministry of Education to instruct all provinces, cities, and counties to send sports achievement products to the current All-China Games for display. (5) Request the Ministry of Education to instruct all universities in the country to earnestly comply with the popularization of university sports. The resolution was passed.

Closing of the Conference: The meeting concluded at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. Chairman Hao Gengsheng announced the adjournment. All the committee members and directors visited the Jiaotong University Gymnasium and then went to the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge for lunch and rest. According to the reporter's investigation, all the committee members and directors returned to their respective hometowns after the meeting.

Draft Regulations: Attached are the draft regulations for sports fields. Article 1: Sports fields are established by provinces, cities, and counties. Article 2: Sports fields established by provinces and cities shall have the following items opened by the provincial and municipal governments and reported to the Ministry of Education for approval and record. Those established by counties and cities shall have the following items opened by the county and city governments and reported to the Provincial Department of Education for approval and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for record: 1. Name, 2. Address, 3. Expenses (divided into start-up and recurring, with the source specified), 4. Regulations, 5. Plan. Sports fields that have already been established must also complete the previous procedures after the promulgation of these regulations. Article 3: Changes and closures of sports fields established by provinces and cities shall be reported by the provincial and municipal governments to the Ministry of Education for approval and record. Those established by counties and cities shall be reported by the county and city governments to the Provincial Department of Education for approval and forwarded to the Ministry of Education for record. Article 4: Sports fields must prepare a budget for the next year and a progress plan one month before the beginning of each year and submit them to the competent educational administrative authority for verification and record. Article 5: Sports fields must prepare a final account for the previous year and a progress overview one month after the end of each year and submit them to the competent educational administrative authority for verification and record. Article 6: Sports fields may set up the following sections: (1) Administrative Section: responsible for documents, accounting, general affairs, etc. (2) Guidance Section: responsible for various sports training organizations and sports competitions research, etc. (3) Promotion Section: responsible for editing, publicity, investigation, statistics, etc. The above sections may be set up in full or merged as appropriate depending on local conditions. Those with a smaller scope may not be divided into sections. Article 7: Provincial sports fields are responsible for guiding the progress of county and city sports fields within the province. If there is more than one provincial sports field, the provincial educational administrative authority shall formulate separate regional guidance measures. Article 8: Sports fields shall have one director who is responsible for overall field affairs. Provincial sports fields shall have qualified personnel selected by the Provincial Department of Education and submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for approval and appointed by the Provincial Government or the Department of Education. Municipal (municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) sports fields shall have qualified personnel selected by the municipal educational administrative authority and submitted to the municipal government for approval and appointment. County and city sports fields shall have qualified personnel selected by the county and city governments and submitted to the Provincial Department of Education for approval and appointment. The director of the sports field shall also serve as the head of one section but may not receive additional salary. Article 9: Each section of the sports field shall have one director and a number of staff members, who shall be selected and appointed by the director of the field and reported to the competent educational administrative authority for record. Article 10: The standard for the allocation of sports field funds is as follows: (1) For annual recurring expenses of more than 20,000 yuan, salaries shall not exceed 50%, and operating expenses shall not be less than 40%. (2) For annual recurring expenses of more than 5,000 yuan, salaries shall not exceed 60%, and operating expenses shall not be less than 32%. (3) For annual recurring expenses of less than 5,000 yuan, salaries shall not exceed 70%, and operating expenses shall not be less than 25%. Article 11: The detailed rules for the operation of sports fields shall be determined by the director of the field and submitted to the competent educational administrative authority for approval and record. Article 12: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

The Tonghua Football Team Scheduled to Embark for Korea: A Group of Nineteen Will Depart on the Nagasaki Maru on the 15th; The Schedule of Three Matches in Korea Is Set Before Touring Japan 183

The Pyongyang Sports Association of Korea, hearing that the Tonghua Football Team was dominating Shanghai, sent a telegram inviting them to Korea for a match. All hospitality will be borne by the Pyongyang Sports Association. Tonghua has agreed and is scheduled to set sail on the 15th for a long expedition. The situation is described as follows:

Expedition Players: The Tonghua players for the Korean expedition have been selected: Li Ning, Guan Xun'an, Feng Yunyou, Li Yichen, Gu Shangquan, Chen Hongguang, Chen Jiaqiu, Dai Linjing, Wan Xianghua, Chen Gongyu, Zhang Jinhai, Ding Zhaocheng, Feng Yunhe, Yin Zhengda, Cao Qiuting, Shen Guoquan, and Jia Youliang, with Lu Zhong'en as the team captain. The list has been submitted to the Pyongyang Sports Association for verification.

Scheduled Departure: The Pyongyang Sports Association's hospitality for the Tonghua Football Team is very generous. It has approved an expense of 4,000 yuan for all the team members' travel expenses. Whether traveling by water, land, or wheels, and hotels, all team members will be in first-class accommodations. The transportation ships and vehicles will also charge half price. Yesterday, the association entrusted the local International Tourist Agency to book nineteen first-class tickets on the Nagasaki Maru of the Japan Mail Steamship Company. They are scheduled to board the ship at the Huishan Wharf at 3:00 PM on the 15th and set sail from Shanghai.

Three Matches: The Tonghua Football Team will play a total of three matches with the football team of the Pyongyang Sports Association in Pyongyang. It is scheduled that the team will depart from Shanghai by ship on the 15th, arrive in Busan on the 17th, and arrive in Pyongyang on the same day. The first match will be held on the 18th. The team will rest for one day in Korea on the 19th and then play the second match on the 20th. The third match will be played on the 21st. After the three matches, the team will go to Seoul. The team will depart from Korea on the 28th, take a connecting ship from Shimonoseki to Japan, and arrive in Tokyo on the 30th.

Touring Japan: After arriving in Tokyo on the 30th, the team will stay and tour Japan. It is scheduled to visit Ueno Park and Kyoto and Nara from the 30th. If the Japanese football community requests a friendly match, the team will also agree to play one match. On May 2nd, the team will go to Osaka and then to Kobe and take a ship back to China. It is estimated that the team will return to Shanghai at 3:00 PM on the 4th. The football team's expedition to Korea, including the tour of Japan, will take approximately three weeks, a total of twenty-one days.

Wang Yunwu's Speech: Wang Yunwu on Methods of Reading 191

The National Reading Movement Conference, sponsored by the China Cultural Construction Association, was held yesterday for the third day. Mr. Wang Yunwu, General Manager of the Commercial Press, was specially invited to speak on methods of reading. Tomorrow (the 11th), starting at 3:15 PM, the Association has specially invited Mr. Cai Yuanpei, a renowned figure in academic circles, to give a speech at the China and West Radio Station on how to study philosophy. The full text of Mr. Wang Yunwu's speech on methods of reading is recorded below:

Methods of Reading: Today, I am honored to be invited by the Cultural Construction Association to speak on methods of reading. Regarding this issue, scholars hold quite different views. Some believe that if one has an interest in reading, there is nothing one cannot read, and no method is needed. Others say that reading without a method is like sailing without a compass, drifting aimlessly in the vast sea, unable to reach the destination. I believe both views have merit, and that interest and method are complementary, not contradictory. Having an interest naturally leads to finding appropriate methods, and having methods makes it easier to generate interest. However, whether to start with method or with interest is worth considering. I believe that if one starts with interest, the first question is how to,

Stir Up Interest: The second question is how long it takes to find appropriate methods after stirring up interest. As for starting with method, it is much simpler. As long as someone provides guidance on appropriate methods, one can follow them and soon develop an interest. Once interest arises, it may even lead to finding better methods. Now, let me give a personal example. In my youth, I was stimulated by my environment and unwilling to submit to it, so I felt an interest in reading. But at that time, I had absolutely no idea about reading methods. I fumbled and stumbled, and although I read a lot of books, I took many detours. To be more specific, many friends know that thirty years ago, I did something extremely foolish, which was to read the entire Encyclopedia Britannica from cover to cover. The Encyclopedia Britannica contains many disciplines, with vastly different natures. What good does it do for a person to read it all? Not only may one not fully understand it, but even if one understands and remembers everything, it only broadens one's general knowledge a little. If one could use the same time and energy, following a

Suitable Procedure: To focus on reading books in one category, the achievement would increase many times over. Moreover, because I started with such a foolish thing, in the following twenty years or so, although I read many books, it was merely expanding on the Encyclopedia Britannica. So, after reading for twenty or thirty years, I had virtually no expertise. It was only in recent years that I realized my mistake and focused on studying one or two subjects. If I had discovered this ten years earlier, I might have achieved more. In short, I developed an interest in reading thirty years ago, but I only found a method of reading in recent years. Because I have suffered from this, I strongly advise everyone to pay attention to methods when starting to read. Now, let me discuss

My Propositions: On methods of reading, I believe that doing scholarship is like building a house: one must first lay the foundation and then start building. The foundation of scholarship is undoubtedly literacy and knowledge of various general subjects. Assuming a level equivalent to the current junior high school graduation as the standard, one can start building on this foundation, in other words, one can start a systematic study. To be more specific, one can choose a subject of interest and read extensively on it. But how can one stir up the interest in reading and develop the habit of continuous reading in the future? I believe the best way is to choose a central question from the beginning and write a systematic manuscript or a systematic paper. This manuscript or paper is not for printing and publication but as a personal account of reading. In the past, scholars advocated making notes, which is indeed a good method, but the nature of notes is disorganized, and their structure is scattered. Although they can help with memory and writing practice, they cannot cultivate

Research Habits: And interests. Conversely, if one can choose a central topic and write a systematic paper, reading will have a purpose, and one will naturally turn to related books and magazines to search for materials. If one finds sufficient material, it is like finding gold in the sand, and the joy is unimaginable. If one does not find sufficient material, it is like craving food when hungry or craving drink when thirsty, and the desire is intense. Originally, the purpose of the graduation thesis written by senior students in universities is like this, but unfortunately, major universities in the country do not pay much attention to this and go through the motions, so the effect is not significant. I have often thought that not only university students should put ten times more effort into writing a deeply researched graduation thesis each, but also high school students should each write a graduation thesis of at least 50,000 words, and even junior high school students should write a thesis of 20,000 to 30,000 words. Because doing such a thesis requires reading more books, practicing writing, and organizing thoughts. Those who study a specialized field can certainly explore specialized issues, while ordinary students can also gather information on simple issues and engage in

Systematic Narration: Now I can advise those who are not studying in schools, if they are interested in continuing to read, it is best to choose a central topic at random. These central topics, big ones are world events and national politics, secondary ones are philosophical problems and scientific principles, small ones are like Peking duck, and nearby ones are like the City God Temple in Shanghai, can all be used as research topics. In particular, the smaller the topic, the more likely it is to arouse interest in reading. However, when starting research, it is best to ask a researcher to give him a rough guide to the research procedure and the materials that should be collected. After a considerable amount of research, he will naturally and automatically search for materials. Now the Cultural Construction Association has invited many experts to select the books that young people who aspire to read should read, just as they have laid the foundation of knowledge for everyone. How to start building on this foundation depends on your own choices and plans. I advise you all to pre-select a topic each, based on this topic, first seek information from the designated books, and you will all develop an interest in the books you read. At the same time, if you have extra energy, you will naturally seek more information on the questions in other books. In this way, your architectural structure in the field of study you are pursuing can be completed sooner rather than later due to intense interest. The end.

Chen Heqin Discusses Again: The Pros and Cons of Phonetic Symbols and Chinese Characters 198

Chen Heqin has published talks in various newspapers on the issue of phonetic symbols and Chinese characters. After the North China News Agency issued Mr. Ge Lijinxi's interpretation of Chen's four opinions on the 1st of this month, Chen made the following remarks:

(1) Mr. Ge believes that phonetic symbols are symbols for recognizing characters, just like punctuation marks. This analogy does not seem very appropriate. In terms of form, punctuation marks are nothing more than a dot or a line, unlike the numerous and varied changes of phonetic symbols. In terms of quantity, they are only used once per sentence or per clause, and are not attached to the side of each character. Generally, punctuation marks are placed below the characters and are not attached to the side of the characters. Therefore, punctuation marks are clearly different from characters, while phonetic symbols are bound to be confused with characters. When reading, looking at two kinds of symbols at the same time, characters and phonetic symbols, takes more time, which is undeniable.

(2) According to my investigation of Japanese newspapers, only one or two out of ten characters are annotated with Kana, which is not comparable to Mr. Ge's proposal to annotate each Chinese character with ancient symbols. It is also said that Japanese newspapers annotate Kana even in six-point type, but the so-called six-point type is definitely not for children to read. If children's books and textbooks are also the same, I am afraid that Mr. Ge cannot guarantee that they will not all become nearsighted.

(3) Attention can only be focused on one point, which is generally recognized by psychologists. If phonetic symbols and Chinese characters are listed side by side, if you only look at Chinese characters when reading, phonetic symbols are useless. If you look at both at the same time and pay attention at the same time, time-consuming, disturbing, and various errors will occur, which will have a great impact on the teaching process.

(4) Mr. Ge also believes that research is needed before implementation. However, there is no shortage of universities with complete equipment and experts with rich experience in the country. Appropriate plans can be used for practical research. If we do not conduct factual experiments first and rashly use tens of millions of children across the country as experimental products, the price may be too high.

(5) During my trip to Singapore this time, I personally saw that the teachers and students of overseas Chinese schools can all speak fluent Mandarin, which is very different from the past when Cantonese and Fujianese translators were needed. Mr. Pan Gongzhan, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, also had the same feeling during his trip to Nanyang to investigate education in the Philippines. However, overseas Chinese in Nanyang did not read textbooks with phonetic symbols and characters side by side before. In fact, all the credit goes to the teachers in schools who teach Mandarin. It can be seen that unifying Mandarin and unifying pronunciation all depend on the efforts of competent teachers, and not on the superfluous phonetic symbols and Chinese characters.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Contributions

Beware of Pickpockets 201

— Yang An

Mr. Zhang Boling said: "The first point in saving the country is to purchase and use domestic goods." The relationship between domestic goods and the national lifeline is generally recognized. Mr. Zhang came from North China and, seeing the prevalence of Japanese goods in North China, suffered endless spiritual pain. Therefore, he advised people to purchase and use domestic goods as the first point in saving the country. If one cannot use domestic goods, are they qualified to talk about saving the country, to do work to save the country? But North China is like this, and the situation in the South is getting worse day by day. Student National Goods Year has been silent since its opening. The waves of advocating domestic goods have also quieted down like hibernation. Various domestic goods factories are struggling desperately under the cold faces of firms. On the other hand, the activities of Japanese merchants are secretly creeping in like pickpockets. This newspaper carried a news item on the 9th about the activities of Japanese merchants in China. In order to develop trade with China and promote the sale of Japanese goods, Japanese manufacturers in Osaka and major merchants have jointly organized 26 manufacturers of hardware, machinery, electrical materials, stationery, fountain pens, book materials, pumps, engines, groceries, oil paper, cosmetics, waterproof materials, automobiles, phonographs, and mining businesses, who will come to China to inspect Shanghai, Nanjing, and the Yangtze River area. The aim is to see what kind of goods China needs and then prepare Japanese goods to be sold in China. Therefore, the Yangtze River liners of Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, which had been suspended, have now resumed service one after another, and there is a great trend to restore the prosperity before January 28th. I don't know if people who advocate domestic goods are moved by this news? They are inspecting, holding meetings, and creeping in secretly, gaining an inch. We are still only knowing selfishness, being muddle-headed, half-senile, and not asking or hearing. What is the intention, what is the heart?

National Goods and Industrial and Technological Salvation 202

— Bei Qiu

More than ten years ago, the four flower tiles of "spring, summer, autumn, and winter" in mahjong seemed to have been cancelled. Whenever the tiles were turned over, it was always "Recovering Rights" or "Revitalizing Industry". At that time, these eight characters could be seen in newspapers every day, people often talked about these eight characters, and people's letters all contained these eight characters. These eight characters were really popular for a while, almost more modern than the two characters "modern" are now!

Until now - taking the Women's National Goods Year as an example, I feel that people's hearts have changed greatly. People love to use foreign goods, letters love to write foreign words, what Paris perfume, what foreign face powder, what... what..., all of this has alarming import surplus figures!

So Mr. Wu Zhihui loudly called out: "Industrial and Technological Salvation!" This means that if our industry and technology can be as developed as those of foreign countries, so that Chinese people can use their own things themselves and do not have to rely on foreign goods, then China can be saved. However, can industry and technology really save the country? We see that the use of electricity in China has been very developed, such as electric facial massages, electric hair perms, electric executions, etc. Who can say that this is for saving the country! This is just a waste of electricity!

Of course, there are also proper uses of electricity, such as electric fans, which can change the climate and make a great contribution to mankind. Moreover, electric fans with this trademark are already popular all over the world. They have been to India, Africa, and the South Seas. They have indeed won a ray of dawn for the Chinese national industrial community, and at the same time, they have fulfilled their obligations to save the country.

Comparing these two, the conclusion is more obvious. Developing industry and technology cannot necessarily save the country, but developing industry and technology can indeed save the country. This is to see what kind of industry and technology is developed. If the development of a kind of industry and technology that is useless to mankind cannot save the country, if the development of an industry and technology that is beneficial to mankind, such as the Hua Sheng electric fan, can save the country.

However, things are not entirely good. If the Hua Sheng electric fan does not have so many types - shaking fans, circulating table fans, wooden blade circulating ceiling fans, circulating air blowers, train fans, etc.: if the Hua Sheng electric fan does not have so many advantages - it only uses 75 watts of electricity per hour (16-inch shaking table fan), and it can rotate more than 1,250 revolutions per minute, and it will not burn even after being opened for the longest time, and at the same time, the price is cheap; if electricity does not have the above two conditions, foreign electric fans will definitely replace it and will never let its footprints spread all over the world.

Therefore, under the slogan of "Industrial and Technological Salvation", we should pay attention to the fact that we must develop industry and technology that is beneficial to mankind, and we must develop industry and technology to the point where foreign goods cannot compete. Only such industry and technology is worthy of being called "Industrial and Technological Salvation" or "Saving Industry and Technology"!

How to Make "Student National Goods Year" Emit Great Power? 203

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

This year is the "Student National Goods Year"! Everyone already knows this. But how can we make this "Student National Goods Year" emit great power? Few people have discussed this. Now I will not hesitate to talk about this issue.

(1) In terms of the family: I think that the position of "students" in the family is "children". Those who instruct children are parents. This is something that teachers cannot reach. Then, parents should understand this point. Their children are "students" in school anyway. Now that it is "Student National Goods Year", they should "lead by example" everywhere and instruct their children to use "domestic goods".

(2) In terms of the school: Children are "students" in school. Those who instruct students are teachers. Naturally, parents cannot control this. In other words, parents have completely delegated the responsibility of instructing their children to the teachers. Then, the teachers should understand this point even more. Since this year is the "Student National Goods Year" and they are in a position to instruct students, they should "lead by example" everywhere and instruct their students to use "domestic goods".

I think that if the parents and teachers can really recognize their responsibilities and work together according to the above methods, instructing and supervising each other at all times, then this "Student National Goods Year" will emit great power - the reasons are also the following two.

(1) In this way, students can have a deep impression of "domestic goods" in their minds, so that they will not forget it as soon as they turn around, and then they can gradually transfer their belief in "foreign goods" to "domestic goods" and use "domestic goods" forever.

(2) It must be known that "Student National Goods Year" is just a "year number" of the national goods movement, and the responsibility of using "domestic goods" is not just limited to students. The practical significance is still that people from all walks of life need to work hard. If, as mentioned above, the instructing methods can be truly "leading by example" for parents and instructing their children to use "domestic goods", then all walks of life can be reached. Because the parents of students are not necessarily people in the academic world, farmers, industrialists, and businessmen can all "lead by example", which means that everyone can use "domestic goods". Isn't this power even greater? Alas! In short, I hope everyone works hard!

Worth Introducing Educational Toys 204

— Jin Shui

Children are the future masters of the entire nation, the most important fundamental elements in organizing a people. Therefore, all countries attach extreme importance to children's education. The stronger the country, the more perfect the children's education. Unlike the casual treatment of children common in our country, with people thinking children's actions are insignificant, even believing that reading, writing, and all other training are merely "little monks chanting scriptures, without sincerity." Thus, they are never corrected, always thinking that when the time comes when they are needed, they will strive to improve. This view is a great mistake. We should understand that children allowed to be indulgent from a young age will "form habits naturally," and even at a considerable age, it will not be easy to change. As the saying goes, "What is meant at three lasts till old age," which is the principle.

Now, our country is gradually paying more attention to children's education. The "Children's Year," which has been shouted for a long time, will finally open under the leadership of the government in early August of this year. This is certainly good news for children across the country. However, we know that whenever a year is designated for something, there must be a task for that year. The mission and task of Children's Year are, of course, to seek happiness for children nationwide. For children, it is to improve their lives, eliminate all bad habits, and shape all children nationwide into complete individuals of the future.

To accomplish this mission of "Children's Year," the only way to start is through education. However, children's education, in addition to books, still needs the assistance of play, because children's lives are mostly about play. Therefore, we should guide children through play, educate children through play. This requires appropriate "toys."

Since toys occupy such an important position in children's education, toys suitable for education have emerged. Here, the reporter wants to introduce a factory specializing in the production of educational toys—the China Educational Toy Factory. Their products are suitable for the purpose of children's education everywhere, capable of directly or indirectly influencing children's emotions, thoughts, character, as well as training in knowledge and skills. Now, the factory's various products are classified and recorded below for selection by the education community or parents.

(1) Transportation: cars, trams, trains, etc.

(2) Military: tanks, armored vehicles, airplanes, small cannons, etc.

(3) Animals: chickens pecking rice, dancing ducks, seals, etc.

(4) Musical Instruments: copper drums, trumpets, rattles, jingles, etc.

(5) Utensils: cookware, fragrant baskets, lead buckets, ticket holders, etc.

Although only a few categories are listed above, they include everything. Each item suits children's psychology. Whether boys or girls, they can arouse interest, inspire wisdom, and are made of sturdy iron, durable to play with. Hygiene, safety, and economy are all taken into consideration. This is not the reporter exaggerating his promotion, but because the materials are excellent, the thinking is precise, and it contributes to children's education, it is indeed worth introducing.

In the past six months, the total number of foreign toy imports was 292,195 gold units, equivalent to 577,962 yuan in national currency. Now that we have such excellent domestic toys, perhaps we can reduce some leakage. This is what the reporter eagerly hopes for.

Domestic Goods Industry and Finance 205

— Meng Zhao

The new initiatives decided by the Shanghai financial community this year are: (1) no foreign rice financing; (2) no credit loans for merchants purchasing foreign goods, especially those selling luxury goods. This is truly an awakening of the financial industry.

The result of years of import surplus is the withering of people's livelihoods. In rural areas and cities, almost all face the danger of not being able to survive today. The only key lies in the large-scale dumping of foreign goods, and the constant westward flow of silver, leading to today's dangerous situation. Although the blame lies with the import merchants' greed for profit, and consumers' drinking poison to quench their thirst! But indirectly facilitating import merchants, promoting economic aggression by powerful countries, and self-depriving the nation's wealth, can the financial industry, which controls the power to regulate surpluses and deficits, evade its responsibility?

My friend Mr. Wang Chusheng, in the article "New Initiatives of the Financial Industry" in the Shanghai Money Industry Monthly, Volume 15, Number 3, has many alarming words. He said, "In recent years, there are more imports and fewer exports. Thus, it is only a one-sided work, which is to pay for the goods for the importers, but cannot absorb foreign capital for the exporters. Under this kind of abnormal state, the financial community is like a bird's nest on a dangerous curtain, how can it last long. Even though issuing loans is one of the business of the bank, the power to examine and choose is controlled by the bank. How can we just chase profit and give convenience to the importers, so as to help foreigners' economic aggression. Although I don't kill Boren, Boren dies because of me." Mr. Wang also made two hopes: (1) All merchants purchasing foreign goods will not be given loans, regardless of whether they sell luxury goods or not; (2) The banking industry and the money industry should stand on the same front and take the same steps. Then, even if the merchants purchasing foreign goods want to sell goods for foreigners, their power is just so-so. The words are truly accurate.

As a member of the domestic goods industry, I urgently hope that our domestic goods industry will jointly support the new initiatives of the financial industry, and move forward hand in hand! And for the future of our domestic goods, open a new opportunity, especially hope that the gentlemen in the financial industry, those who talk should get up and act.
